# Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Restore the Dark Brotherhood's sanctuary.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary"), [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | Refurnished Sanctuary |
| ID: | DarkBrotherhoodSanctuaryRepair |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") | **Next →** [Take the Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_the_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Take the Hidden Treasure") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") | | → Next | [Take the Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_the_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Take the Hidden Treasure") | | |

Interior of the furnished [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") in the new [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
2. Speak to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory").
3. Purchase the upgrades.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will instruct you to go and speak to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") about restoring the newly reacquired [Dawnstar Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary"). Travel to The Ragged Flagon and speak to Delvin. He is more than happy to restore anything you want for the prices listed below.

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| 1000 gold | | 5000 gold | | 5000 gold | | 5000 gold | | 3000 gold | |
| 22 new banners around the Sanctuary | | 1 Alchemy Lab  [Lotus Extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Lotus_Extract "Skyrim:Lotus Extract") x2    Garden of regrowing ingredients:  [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") x2; [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") x2; [Giant Lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") x3; [Swamp Fungal Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") x2; [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") x3; [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") x2; [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") x3.    Several ingredients on the Alchemy Lab table, including:    [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust") x2; [Falmer Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear") x2; [Human Flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh") x2; [River Betty](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty") x3 | | Adds four [torture victims](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Victim "Skyrim:Torture Victim") to the Sanctuary, hung by their wrists. Each of these four victims [reveals the location](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_the_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Take the Hidden Treasure") of treasure after being prompted. | | Adds a secret entrance and exit on the other side of Dawnstar. [(map)](http://srmap.uesp.net/?locx=25023&locy=102150&zoom=15&search=Dawnstar%20Sanctuary) | | Adds a personal master bedroom, including dressers, weapon racks, chests and a bed. Also adds [Tumblerbane Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumblerbane_Gloves "Skyrim:Tumblerbane Gloves"). Bedroom also includes mannequin for display of clothing. | |

After buying all the upgrades, talking to Delvin Mallory once more about the Dawnstar Sanctuary will complete the quest. You will have just 1,000 gold left of your previous reward after purchasing all of the upgrades.

## Bugs

- Even after you have fully upgraded the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary"), your quest log may not update and still tell you to "Employ Delvin Mallory's services".
  - To fix this, visit the sanctuary and then return to Delvin, and ask to upgrade the Sanctuary more, at which point he will tell you there is nothing else he can do and you will complete the quest.

## Quest Stages

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DarkBrotherhoodSanctuaryRepair stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DarkBrotherhoodSanctuaryRepair`.

The Night Mother

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Hide in the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")'s coffin and listen to [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero").
2. Step out and confront Cicero and [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid").
3. Take contracts from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").

### Secret Agent

After returning from your assassination mission in [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes"), Astrid will confide that she needs help with a matter of a somewhat more personal nature. She confesses that she is a little concerned about the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")'s Keeper, [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero"). The strange and erratic jester has been locking himself in the chamber with the Night Mother's coffin and frantically whispering to someone. Astrid fears a conspiracy and asks you to spy on Cicero to see what he is up to. However, in order to effectively eavesdrop and not be detected she asks you to hide in the coffin with the Night Mother's corpse. You can state your objections or remain silent at this strange directive, but in either case, make your way to the chamber to make yourself cozy with the Night Mother.

The Night Mother speaks

You can talk to the other Dark Brotherhood members about [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid")'s conspiracy theory. You can tell them: *"Astrid thinks a Family member may be conspiring with Cicero."*

They all answer differently:

[Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn"): *"She said that? If I find anyone working against my wife, or this [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), I'll beat them to death with their own severed head. Of course, they'd probably already be dead... But you know what I mean!"*

[Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette"): *"Oh! Well, I hope she doesn't suspect me. I mean, I've spoken with Cicero a bit, and he's quite charming. But I'd never go against Astrid. Never."*

[Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex"): *" Ha! And would that surprise anyone? This Sanctuary's a mess. Wouldn't surprise me if somebody's talking to the fool on the sly. Making deals. And no, before you ask, it's not me. I know which side my bread is buttered on."*

[Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella"): *"To what end? Usurping Astrid's authority as leader of the Sanctuary? Hmmm... Yes, I can see her concern. Thank you for bringing this to my attention."*

[Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"): *"Does she? Listen, brother/sister... Astrid is my mistress, and I worship the ground she walks on. But this Cicero business has her a bit... paranoid."*

[Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara"): *"You're joking. While I can understand if some family members wish to honor the [Old Ways](/wiki/Lore:Dark_Brotherhood "Lore:Dark Brotherhood") once more, surely no one would oppose Astrid's rule."*

There is no option for asking Cicero, as this would ruin Astrid's plan.

### Listen to Your Mother

You will need to pick the novice lock on the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")'s coffin, then step inside. The scene fades to black and you will soon hear Cicero begin to address someone. He pleads for his companion to speak, and complains that he must do all the work, but is ever obedient. Suddenly, you will see the Night Mother in the coffin with you; she begins to speak and you realize that she pities Cicero. He has been attempting to communicate with the Night Mother all along, however the Night Mother refuses to speak to Cicero because he is not the Listener. Outside the coffin, Cicero despairs of the Night Mother actually speaking to anyone, and at his failure at finding a Listener. Again, the Night Mother addresses you. She names you Listener and tasks you with traveling to [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") and speaking with [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre"). She instructs you to tell Cicero a covert phrase: "Darkness rises when silence dies".

### Darkness Rises When Silence Dies

The coffin opens and as you step out, a horrified Cicero demands an explanation. Tell him you are "the one", but he refuses to believe you. Tell him the signal phrase the Night Mother gave you and Cicero becomes ecstatic and dances a little jig. Astrid will burst into the room, alerted by the commotion. She comes to realize that there is no treachery or traitor, but is a little put-off by your assertion that you are now the Listener. When you explain what the Night Mother has asked of you, Astrid becomes defensive claiming, *"I'm still the leader in this family"*. Astrid needs time to process all of this and sends you to take a contract from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"), rather than allowing you to go to Volunruud, while she thinks about this turn of events. If you have already completed the first three contracts Nazir gave you then he will give you two new contracts, [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern") and [Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk"). If you have not completed the initial contracts, then Nazir will complain that you still have contracts to complete and urge you to get on with them. In either case, this quest will complete upon speaking with Nazir.

## Notes

- Should you choose to disregard Astrid's orders and proceed to Volunruud on your own, you will be able to receive the contract but not act on it until killing at least one of the Nazir's contract targets. You must kill at least one contract target after completing this quest and then return to the sanctuary in order to start [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken"), which will start when Astrid talks to you (before you collect your pay from Nazir).

## Bugs

- If you close the iron door you open to enter the room and enter the tomb, Cicero cannot walk into the room and attempt to speak to the Night Mother, leaving you inside the tomb in mid cut-scene.
  - If you wait an hour in the coffin, Cicero will be placed in the room and the quest will go on as normal.
  -  Open the console, enter `prid 00080E17`, then enter in `unlock`. After that, close the console and wait an hour. The quest will continue as normal after that.
- When Astrid tells you to go talk to Nazir for more side contracts, Nazir may not have any quest options available. This is possibly caused by the targets from Nazir's next contract having already been killed. **?**
  -  Entering `setstage DB04 200` in the console fixes this. This will complete the Whispers in the Dark quest and allow you to get the [next quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") from Astrid. The only thing you will have missed are the two contracts Nazir gives.
  - Deactivate the quest while inside the Sanctuary, exit to the outside, and reactivate the quest. Proceed to follow through with the quest as normal and the bug should be fixed.
  - Skip straight to Volunruud and speak with Amaund Motierre to receive the quest The Silence Has Been Broken. The quest journal will not update and no dialogue options will be given but the quest can be completed via following the walkthrough. The only thing you will have missed are the two contracts Nazir gives and any dialogue.[*verification needed — This worked for PS3-does it work for PC and Xbox as well?*]

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.

- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB04`.

Whistling Mine

**Whistling Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). It contains only one zone, *[Whistling Mine](#Whistling_Mine)*.

The mine is the only consistently inhabited settlement in the [hold of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") besides the city of the same name. All of the miners originally began digging the mine thinking it would make them rich. [Angvid](/wiki/Skyrim:Angvid "Skyrim:Angvid") and [Badnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Badnir "Skyrim:Badnir") seem to have lost their morale, while [Gunding](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunding "Skyrim:Gunding") and [Thorgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorgar "Skyrim:Thorgar") still claim the mine will eventually be successful, possibly through the discovery of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") or [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") ore. Thorgar, the mine's owner, will [buy iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Whistling Mine Residents

| Whistling Mine |
| --- |
| [Angvid](/wiki/Skyrim:Angvid "Skyrim:Angvid")  [Badnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Badnir "Skyrim:Badnir")  [Gunding](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunding "Skyrim:Gunding")  [Thorgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorgar "Skyrim:Thorgar") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The mine lies along the southern road between Winterhold and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), at the base of the mountains. A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is just outside and to the right of the entrance, with three pieces of owned [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") on a crate beside it. Two sacks can be found next to the crate. A [Winterhold guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Guard "Skyrim:Winterhold Guard") patrols the road in front of the mine, and there is an [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") encounter just north on the road. A path rising to the west starts just south of the mine and leads to [Mount Anthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor") and the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura"). A [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found down the road north of the mine.

### Whistling Mine

Mine interior

It is one of the smallest mines in Skyrim, containing only two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Upon entering the mine, the first chamber serves as the camp for the four miners. In the center of the chamber is a campfire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand beside it. Four bedrolls are east of the campfire, and a table with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and chairs is to the north. To the west of the table are a couple of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, one with a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Heavy Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Heavy Armor Forging")*, while a coin purse rests on a hay bale nearby. There are several other food sacks and barrels around the chamber. To the west is an ice tunnel that leads to a second chamber with a wooden ramp up to the two iron ore veins on the north wall.

## Notes

- The Winterhold guard who patrols the road near Whistling Mine is the only one who can be seen with the [Winterhold Guard's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Winterhold Guard's Shield"), as the guards in the city of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") don't carry it due to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold#Notes "Skyrim:Winterhold").

## Bugs

- When using USSEP, the Winterhold guard who patrols the road near Whistling Mine may have two Winterhold Guard's Shields, holding one and having another one in his/her inventory.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, addresses this issue. The inventory copy has been removed. This was missed during the USKP 1.2.4 fix which took place back in 2012.

## Maps

- 

  Whistling Mine

# Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow

## Overview

White Ridge Barrow

**White Ridge Barrow** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") in the northern part of Solstheim inhabited by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiders "Skyrim:Spiders"). It contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for part of the [Cyclone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyclone "Skyrim:Cyclone") shout, the dragon priest [Dukaan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dukaan_(creature) "Skyrim:Dukaan (creature)"), the *[Black Book: The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")*, and an [imbuing chamber](#Imbuing_Chamber) in which you can create [spider scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Scrolls "Skyrim:Spider Scrolls").

It contains two zones: *[White Ridge Barrow](#White_Ridge_Barrow)* and *[White Ridge Sanctum](#White_Ridge_Sanctum)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book (quest)")**: Retrieve a Black Book from a dungeon.
- **[Black Book: The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Lost Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knowledge "Skyrim:Lost Knowledge")**: Retrieve the [Black Books](/wiki/Lore:Black_Book "Lore:Black Book") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Backdoor to the imbuing chamber

The exterior of the main entrance is fairly devoid of features. There is a single [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush and an open ice field in front of the barrow. To the south is a stream flowing south from under White Ridge Barrow. Farther to the south is an unmarked shack, with two glowing blue eggs outside containing [jumping frost spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Jumping_Frost_Spider_(item) "Skyrim:Jumping Frost Spider (item)") and an [albino spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"). Behind and to the west of the shack are two [sapphire geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Geode "Skyrim:Sapphire Geode"). Inside the shack is an [albino spider egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Albino Spider Pod") and a trap door leading directly to the imbuing chamber; however, the door is locked ([key](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar%27s_Cage_Door_Key "Skyrim:Merilar's Cage Door Key") required). The key can be collected from the interior of White Ridge Barrow, making access to the imbuing chamber far easier on return trips. In front of the iron door into the barrow, there is blood splatter on the ground. The barrow is due west of [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow") and east of the [Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source").

### White Ridge Barrow

First room

You'll enter into a small room with two dead [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"), one of them slouched against a barred wooden door straight ahead. There are two bed rolls on the right, and a chest in the northwest corner. Remaining items in the room are a few bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and some food and eating implements on a long table. A smaller table to the left holds two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") to the left next to a pile of firewood.

Lift the bar and open the door to find a dead reaver on the other side, and proceed down the stairs ahead. You'll pass another two reavers and two albino spiders, all dead. Take care of two further living spiders, loot the egg on the left side of the passage, and proceed to a fork ahead. Both directions lead to a door on the opposite side; however, taking the right fork, there is another spider egg on your right, and an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") growing by the outer wall. Through a door to the left at the back of the circular passage, you'll find skeletal remains at the top of a wooden spiral staircase, along with an iron dagger, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Continue down the staircase past more and more spiderwebs. At the bottom, there is a corridor heading east, with two dead albino spiders and an albino spider egg on the left-hand side. You'll pass another dead reaver with a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") beside him on the floor just before entering a large web-filled room containing a [flame cloaked spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Cloaked_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Flame Cloaked Spider (creature)") and more albino spiders. To the left side of the room are two [ruby geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Geode "Skyrim:Ruby Geode") with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") in front of them, and two glowing red egg sacs that will release flame cloaked spiders to the right of the geodes. On the right side near the southwest corner is an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), and to the southeast is another red glowing egg sac containing a flame cloaked spider. There are two albino spider eggs by two pillars. In the center of the room is a platform containing two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). Another large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") sits behind the stone benches to the right of the platform. To the left behind the benches is another albino spider, and among some bones are copies of *[Amongst the Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Amongst_the_Draugr "Skyrim:Amongst the Draugr")* and *[Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Harvesting_Frostbite_Spider_Venom "Skyrim:Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom")*.

Ancient equipment

You'll find a pull chain ahead which lowers a drawbridge in front of you when activated. The bridge itself isn't helpful quite yet, as another drawbridge is still raised in a room across from you, but you can use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") to make it to the far side; aim for the right of the raised bridge, as this is where the gap is. You can also reach the far side with careful jumping by landing on the support log between the two halves of the bridge, then jumping from there to the right side with the gap. Whichever method you employ, use the pull chain on the far platform, which features an empty [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem") in an unlit brazier to the north and a chest next to the chain, to lower the other half of the bridge. Head back across the bridge and descend either staircase to the room's lower level. Kill the reaver patrolling here. There is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus growing against the southeast wall, and two albino spider eggs against the same wall farther to the south. In the southern corner is a table in shallow water holding an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet") and a [honed ancient Nord greatsword of Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Ancient_Nord_Greatsword_of_Cold "Skyrim:Honed Ancient Nord Greatsword of Cold"), with a pair of [ancient Nord boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Boots "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Boots") beside it. Beware the flame cloaked spider which may burst from its egg sac if you come too close.

Another staircase at the north side of the room leads up to a new area. Loot the large urn to the right before arriving at what appears to be a dead end. Destroy some thick spiderwebs ahead of you to reveal an iron door, behind which is another room containing two albino spiders and their eggs. There are some [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushrooms "Skyrim:Glowing Mushrooms") on the walls, and the bodies of three skeletons and two draugr nearby. When you come close enough to the back of the chamber, a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") will awaken from its sarcophagus. After defeating it, loot the two unlocked chests, one on each side of the room. You can go no further here, so head back to the large chamber to the south toward the table in shallow water and continue around the corner to the west.

To the west is a reaver, a [jumping flame spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Jumping_Flame_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Jumping Flame Spider (creature)"), and two red glowing spider eggs that will burst when you approach to release two more jumping flame spiders. The eggs are on a raised area with two open sarcophagi, one in each corner, with the two dead draugr lying on the ground nearby. Head down the corridor ahead and turn left, watching out for a flame cloaked spider which hides in its egg in the tiny room on the right. Kill an albino spider in the corridor on the left and harvest the [damaged albino spider pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Damaged_Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Damaged Albino Spider Pod") from the egg on the left. Continue onward, turning left again at the end of the hallway. Mine the two ruby geodes and two [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") deposits, and continue forward to kill another flame cloaked spider before reaching the entrance to the next zone.

### White Ridge Sanctum

Merilar Rendas

Proceed down the first hallway. Ahead is a pile of rubble with an unlit brazier on top, inside which is a pickaxe and two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"). On your right just before the brazier are two draugr corpses lying in front of a barred wooden door. Prepare yourself for an onslaught in the following huge chamber, where several enemies await: two reavers, two flame cloaked spiders, and [Merilar Rendas](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar_Rendas "Skyrim:Merilar Rendas"), a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") sorcerer who carries six flame cloaked spiders and six jumping flame spiders in her inventory. [Her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Merilar's Journal") contains information about the spiders and some clues as to what you may find ahead. Take the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar%27s_Cage_Door_Key "Skyrim:Merilar's Cage Door Key") from her body and continue on.

Albino spiders

In the northeast corner of the chamber, you'll find an imp stool growth beneath a wooden ramp leading up to a room containing the most notable feature in White Ridge Sanctum: the [imbuing chamber](#Imbuing_Chamber). There are seven albino spiders in the room at the top of the ramp, as well as four red glowing eggs that spawn jumping flame spiders. At the top of the ramp, on your left is a dead reaver and two ruby geodes. To the right is another dead reaver, and farther to the right, slightly behind you, is one of the red glowing eggs. Two more glowing eggs are to the east under a wooden bridge. The albino spiders are wandering all over the room and will investigate any fighting. The fourth glowing egg is on the wooden structure, to your right as you enter, by the beginning of the wooden bridge. A third ruby geode rests beneath the supports of the bridge in the room's eastern corner, and a third dead reaver rests near an adept-locked cage door to the north. Behind the door is a mass of spider webs, blocking the path.

Use the key you took from Merilar to open the door, and hack or burn through the thick webbing beyond. The corridor turns to the east, with a barred wooden door on your left. First proceed to the end of the hallway and turn left to find a chest. You may hear a reaver yelling for help, so prepare yourself. Through the barred door await four [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and two albino spiders in a small room. Dispatch them (runes cast near the base of the door, without unbarring it, can be a safe and effective technique), loot the three albino spider eggs, then backtrack to the other side of the cage door you came through.

The bedroom

Walk under the supports for the bridge to the southeast side of the room to find what remains of a bedroom, now home to an albino spider and covered in spiderwebs. On the right side of the room, you'll find a bed next to a small table which holds a random book, a random health potion, three loose coins, an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and another copy of the key carried by Merilar. A medium coin purse is on the floor. The bookcase near the foot of the bed holds nine random books, a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), and another random health potion. On the left side of the room, there is another bed and two bookcases. The southern bookcase holds eleven random books, a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"), a leveled extra magicka potion, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and three sacks. The northern bookcase holds nine random books, a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), two [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") (one empty, one filled), and a small sack. There is a leveled extra magicka potion on the floor to the left of this bookcase, and a large coin purse to the right. There are also two albino spider eggs between the two bookcases.

Back in the main cave, at the top of the ramp is an expert-locked cage which can be unlocked with the same key. Inside the cage, you'll find the body of [Servos Rendas](/wiki/Skyrim:Servos_Rendas "Skyrim:Servos Rendas"). [His journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Servos%27_Journal "Skyrim:Servos' Journal") indicates that the four bandits were locked in the room with the spiders as part of experiments he and his sister, Merilar, had been conducting with the spiders. On the table behind him are two damaged albino spider pods, three standard albino spider pods, and two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), while the [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") below contains eight more albino spider pods. The table to the left holds a pickaxe, three rubies, and a copy of Servos' [spider experiment notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Experiment_Notes "Skyrim:Spider Experiment Notes"), next to the imbuing chamber itself. For more information on using the device, see [this section](#Imbuing_Chamber).

Leave the cage and cross the bridge ahead. On the other side, on your left are three sacks and a crate with two random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top, followed by a ladder leading up to a trap door. The trap door exits to Solstheim, placing you in the shack directly south of the main entrance, and requires Merilar's key. Proceed through the tunnel past the ladder to the northeast, where you'll find evidence of previous mining activity. Past a growth of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") on the left, to the right is a knapsack and an open crate containing two [iron ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), one [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), and a leather strip. A ruby geode is to the left of the crate, with another farther along on your left.

Backtrack to the main chamber of White Ridge Sanctum, cross the wooden bridge spanning the chasm with a stream flowing through it, turn to the west, and proceed through the corridor on the west side. On your left, just as you enter the corridor, is a red glowing egg, and on your right are two random soul gems in an iron bowl on the ground. There are also two albino spiders and a glowing red egg containing a flame cloaked spider hidden behind a pillar at the bottom of the first flight of stairs. The corridor turns to the east and descends again into a flooded area, with a chest in the flooded circular room visible from above through a grating in the floor of the main chamber. The path continues to the north to the bottom of the chasm, where four ruby geodes are scattered about. Return to the main chamber once again, taking the stone stairs leading up to the south on your right. At the top of the first flight is a glowing red egg opposite to the east containing a jumping flame spider. Turn to the south and climb another flight of stairs to find some blood splatters, a lamp, and a pickaxe in front of some spider webbing blocking the path. Past the webbing is an empty chamber, with an unlocked iron door surrounded by candles.

Dukaan in front of the word wall

Through the door is a room containing a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for part of the [Cyclone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyclone "Skyrim:Cyclone") shout. As you approach the wall, the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Dukaan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dukaan_(creature) "Skyrim:Dukaan (creature)") will burst from his nearby sarcophagus and attack. Defeat him, loot the chest in front of his sarcophagus, and learn the new word. On the other side of the room, below the stairs by which you entered, is the *[Black Book: The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")*. Reading it will begin the similarly named [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)"), in which you are transported to [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha").

### Imbuing Chamber

The Imbuing Chamber

The Imbuing Chamber device allows you to create [spider scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Scrolls "Skyrim:Spider Scrolls"). These can be equipped in each hand, and are thrown rather than cast. Some [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Experiment_Notes "Skyrim:Spider Experiment Notes") next to the device describe a few recipes, but more can be discovered by experimenting based on the instructions.

To operate, place ingredients in the receptacle, then activate the switch on the front of the device. Recipes for spider creation follow an easy pattern, with albino spider pods and damaged albino spider pods being the core components. The following lists describe additional usable materials and their effects.

**Pods**

- Albino Spider Pods — May be combined with a [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") and (optionally) a salt pile. Regular gems may be replaced with any soul gem or [Dwarven oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Oil "Skyrim:Dwarven Oil"), but salt piles are useless in this combination.
  - **Gem only** — Jumping spider. Jumps at nearest enemy and explodes, dealing elemental damage.
  - **Gem and Salt Pile** — Element-cloaked spider. Follows the player and continuously deals elemental damage to enemies near it.
  - **Soul Gem** — Mind control spider. Attaches to creatures and people, who will then become friendly and fight for you for 30 seconds.
  - **Dwarven Oil** — [Oil spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(item) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (item)").
- Damaged Albino Spider Pods — May only be combined with a gem.
  - **Gem only** — Creates a dead spider that explodes when enemies approach it, dealing elemental damage.

**Gems**
Gems determine the elemental damage of the spiders. Diamonds and garnets have no known use.

- [Amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst") — [Shock cloaked](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Cloaked_Spider_(item) "Skyrim:Shock Cloaked Spider (item)")
- [Emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald") — [Poison cloaked](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison_Cloaked_Spider "Skyrim:Poison Cloaked Spider")
- Ruby — Flame cloaked
- Sapphire — Frost cloaked

**Notes:**

- Imbuing a pod with a standard gem yields three spiders. Flawless gems yield six spiders.
- Imbued spiders will appear under "scrolls" in your inventory.
- There are numerous recipes for creating spiders:

:   | Recipes |
    | --- |
    | - [Recipe - Exploding Flame Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_-_Exploding_Flame_Spider "Skyrim:Recipe - Exploding Flame Spider") - [Recipe - Exploding Flame Spider 2x](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_-_Exploding_Flame_Spider_2x "Skyrim:Recipe - Exploding Flame Spider 2x") - [Recipe - Exploding Frost Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_-_Exploding_Frost_Spider "Skyrim:Recipe - Exploding Frost Spider") - [Recipe - Exploding Frost Spider 2x](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_-_Exploding_Frost_Spider_2x "Skyrim:Recipe - Exploding Frost Spider 2x") - [Recipe - Exploding Poison Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_-_Exploding_Poison_Spider "Skyrim:Recipe - Exploding Poison Spider") - [Recipe - Exploding Poison Spider 2x](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_-_Exploding_Poison_Spider_2x "Skyrim:Recipe - ## Notes

- This location is mentioned in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") during the quest [A Web of Troubles](/wiki/Online:A_Web_of_Troubles "Online:A Web of Troubles"), which explains the origins of the magical spiders.

## Bugs

- When activating the bars on wooden doors, they may not lift, preventing you from proceeding to the next area.
  - Waiting for 48 hours or reloading from the previous zone or cell should resolve this.
- The word wall may appear as though it's already been used, and the animation won't play. Nevertheless, if you stand close to it, you'll obtain the word as expected.
- White Ridge Barrow was assigned the LocTypeAnimalDen keyword instead of the LocTypeDraugrCrypt keyword. This could potentially result in it being chosen as a radiant location for [Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:White River Watch

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: White River Watch ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River+Watch)) | | |

White River Watch

**White River Watch** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[White River Watch](#White_River_Watch)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **Note:** This location is intended to be one of many potential targets for one or more of the radiant quests found on [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant"); however, without patches, it won't be targeted (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

### Exterior

Two bandits are outside the cave. The two bandits positions make it very hard to approach the caves stealthily. The first bandit stands guard near a campfire and overlooks the dirt path, and the second bandit stands higher up, near the entrance to the cave. In the bushes to the left just before the campfire is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). The first bandit carries a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_to_Rodulf "Skyrim:Note to Rodulf") which warns Rodulf to stop making a fool of [Hajvarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Hajvarr_Iron-Hand "Skyrim:Hajvarr Iron-Hand")'s uncle. On the other side of the bushes is a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and on the opposite side of the path is a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower").

There is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging over the campfire. On the table by the campfire is a sprig of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and some cheese. There are a number of crates and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks and barrels around the table and to the left of the entrance. There is a novice-locked chest just north of the fire and a rack holding three whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") to the right. By the cliff face to the south is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), another purple mountain flower and a [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") bush.

### White River Watch

When you enter, [Ulfr the Blind](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfr_the_Blind "Skyrim:Ulfr the Blind") asks you to identify yourself, thinking you are Rodulf, *"Eh? Who's there? Rodulf, that you?"* If you try to pass yourself off as Rodulf, he will advise you to talk to the boss, *"Boss was looking for you - said he'd be up at the summit. Better not keep him waiting."* He will return to "reading" [his book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfr%27s_Book "Skyrim:Ulfr's Book"), which is actually blank. If you talk to him again, he will offer some encouragement, *"Good luck out there."* If you threaten him, he will call out for help, *"Hey! Somebody get down here! Help!"* This will make two bandits spawn in the next room: they will not appear otherwise if it is your first run through, but they will spawn if you return to the cave after killing everyone in it to continue picking up loot.

To the right of the entrance is a pile of food sacks, barrels, and crates. Two of the barrels contain common [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Among the crates are two patches of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus, with two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") hanging from a rack above. By a chair is one patch of each of the following: [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi. A basket on the ground behind Ulfr contains four leeks. The passage continues to the east, passing a small set of shelves holding a [fur cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"). To the right is a barrel with a quiver containing ten [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") and farther to the right is a flight of stairs leading up. Around and behind the stairs are three patches of white cap and two patches of imp stool fungi, a wardrobe, a cupboard holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a few food sacks. At the top of the stairs there is a pile of firewood with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") on top and a barrel of common ingredients beside it. The stairs continue to climb to the northwest, passing a ledge with a small table holding a [fur helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Helmet "Skyrim:Fur Helmet"). There are five more patches of imp stool and four more of white cap fungi in this area.

As you pass through the tunnel to the next section you can overhear the end of a conversation between two rebellious bandits:

:   **Bandit #1**: *"So, you in?"*
:   **Bandit #2**: *"...Yeah. We can't have that rheumy-eyed fool as our watchman, even if he is Hajvarr's uncle. Time we dealt with both of them."*
:   **Bandit #1**: *"We strike tonight, at dusk. Be ready."*

Despite their bravado they never do act on their plans. These two bandits are near the campfire up the slope from the next section, while a third bandit from deeper in the cave will be alerted if hostilities break out. The chamber is split in two with a ramp leading up on the left to the higher level, where all the bandits can be found. In the lower area there are five unowned bedrolls, with a patch of imp stool and one of Namira's rot fungi among them, a partially sunken end table with another fur hat and a [common book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top and a pair of leveled [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") behind. There is a dresser to the south, containing random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), a pair of leveled [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), some [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and eleven loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). The raised area has a campfire on the left, with a small table to the right, holding a bottle of alto wine and a leveled [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"). To the right of the campfire is a food barrel and a cupboard holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a copy of *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* and one of *[The Hope of the Redoran](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hope_of_the_Redoran "Skyrim:The Hope of the Redoran")*, and there is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top. Opposite is a stack of crates and food sacks with a rack hanging to the right, holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). In the southeast corner, beneath a ledge is an unlocked chest.

A ramp leads up to the southeast and a small area containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"): the third bandit previously mentioned was working here, and may still be, if you have been stealthy enough in your approach. On the crate beside the lab is a leveled skill [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). The path heads north through a narrow passage, before opening up into a narrow winding chamber with another cupboard on the right holding a leveled heavy [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). In front of the cupboard is a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), and to the left is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). There is also a patch of each of the following: bleeding crown, [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), imp stool, Namira's rot, and white cap fungi. On the left is a dresser with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and small coin purse on top. As you approach this you will be able to overhear another conversation:

:   **Bandit #3**: *"You think it'll work?"*
:   **Bandit #4**: *"'Course not. Dogs I could train. But a half-starved wolf? Not a chance."*
:   **Bandit #3**: *"Right. Lucky if it doesn't rip our throats out."*

The conversation is between two bandits on the same level of the cave: there are another two bandits in the next room too. One is above the first two, and another is higher up and to the left, but is still within range to be alerted to your presence by the others. You can choose to attack them by yourself, or you can pull a chain on the right-hand wall that releases the aforementioned [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"). This provokes a response by the bandit closest the cage, *"Look out! The wolf is loose!"* This particular wolf is unique: it will attack the bandits first due to a particular [faction](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Prisoner_Faction "Skyrim:White River Prisoner Faction"), but it is still hostile to you.

Under a bush to the left by the entrance to this section is a white cap fungus. Further along are two Namira's rot fungi, and inside the novice-locked cage is a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a patch of imp stool fungus, plus the wolf if you haven't released it. There are a couple of barrels to the right of the cage, one of which holds uncommon ingredients. By the barrels under the rock slope is a blisterwort fungus. The ramp leading up is against the right-hand wall and there is a ledge half way up containing a wooden bench, with an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") to the left, two patches of imp stool, and three of white cap fungi. At the top you'll see a small hanging cage overhanging the chamber below, this is obviously the cage mentioned in the note to Rodulf. There is a dead bandit inside the cage. Carefully climbing down the ledge in front of the cage should allow you to just reach the body which carries the same items as a normal bandit, plus 35 extra gold. On the right of the path is a small set of shelves holding an iron mace, a leveled [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a bottle of alto wine and two bottles of wine.

On the left-hand side of the path is a bleeding crown, and on the right, a white cap, followed by a fly amanita. There is another fly amanita by the wardrobe across the way, and a bleeding crown by the brazier to the left. Beyond the three barrels (two of which hold common ingredients) there is a fly amanitia and bleeding crown fungi. There is also another pickaxe, which is handy for the [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") located here. On a ledge beyond the vein there is a Namira's rot and a fly amanita fungi. The path continues to rise heading north. Along the path upwards there are three bleeding crown on the left, three fly amanita and a bleeding crown fungi on the right.

### Exterior: White River Overlook

The overlook is aptly named, for it overlooks a great portion of the White River. From this area you can see a distance along the road to Whiterun, giving plenty of time to lay an ambush along the road. [Hajvarr Iron-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Hajvarr_Iron-Hand "Skyrim:Hajvarr Iron-Hand") sits in a chair: he has also kept a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hajvarr%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hajvarr's Journal") on some of his thoughts, which he carries with him. He is always hostile and will attack on sight. He also carries the unique [Ironhand Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironhand_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Ironhand Gauntlets"), which are a pair of [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets") with a [fortify two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Two-Handed "Skyrim:Fortify Two-Handed") enchantment.

On the table where Hajvarr sits lies a leveled [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), a leveled [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), and a leveled [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"). If you turn back toward the cave, there is a boss chest and a large coin purse to the left of the wooden steps, and a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush to the right.

You can now either make your way back through the cave, or take the slightly more treacherous path over the rocks. It isn't too difficult to pick a path down if you head north along the rocks. Alternatively, if you have cleared the cave, you can simply fast travel from the overlook instead of backtracking through the cave or scaling the mountainside.

## Notes

- [Eisa Blackthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa_Blackthorn "Skyrim:Eisa Blackthorn") and [Ra'jirr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27jirr "Skyrim:Ra'jirr") are former members of the White River gang. *[Eisa's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eisa's Journal")* describes how they chose to leave and their adventures afterward.
- [Whiterun guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") will alert you to this location with the comment, *"Careful if you cross the river to the east. Old Hajvarr Iron-Hand and his brigands are holed up in that cave, White River Watch."*
- [Carriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage") drivers will also alert you to its location with the comment, *"Got keen eyes? Might see nasty old Hajvarr up on White River Watch. Piece of work. [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") should just run him out and have done with it."*
- If you kill the two bandits that come to Ulfr's aid and then sheathe your weapon, he will stop fighting and return to the table where he was sitting. These two enemies will always be low-level bandits ("Bandit" instead of "Bandit Highwayman", etc.).
- Hajvarr's journal mentions capturing a wolf from some cargo moving down the road, which is likely the wolf inside the cave.
- To access the overlook without going through the cave, you can use a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") to climb the mountain west of [Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp"), then descend carefully to the overlook.

## Bugs

- The hidden quest associated with this location is supposed to ensure the unique NPCs never respawn after being killed. The quest does not shut down properly, however, allowing the NPCs to respawn and leaving this location unavailable for most, if not all, radiant quests that don't specifically target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12158))
- If you do not release the wolf when going through the cave, then exit to the overlook and reenter, the wolf will have spawned outside the door to its cage. It will not be hostile.
  -  Opening the cage either by pulling the chain or picking the lock will turn the wolf hostile again.

# Skyrim:White River

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: White River ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:White_River "Lore:White River")) | | |
| Regions | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| Eastern Skyrim | |

The source of the White River

**White River** is the longest river in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)"), stretching from the south of the province to the northeast corner.

The source of the White River is [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It flows northeast to join the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts") past [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). Along the way, it passes through [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") and near [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River") and [River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim") are the two main tributaries of the White River.

# Skyrim:Whiterun Hold

## Overview

This article is about the hold. For the city, see [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

|  |  |  |
