Whiterun Hold

**Whiterun Hold** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in central [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), with its capital in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is initially neutral in Skyrim's [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), but both sides are actively competing to gain control of Whiterun. As a result, it is the site of the first battle of the war, Battle for Whiterun ([Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")). The Imperial Legion will secure the allegiance of the incumbent Jarl [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"), who seeks reinforcements in the face of an imminent Stormcloak siege, and Balgruuf's government, now aligned with the Empire, will accordingly remain in control of the hold should the Imperial Legion successfully defend the city; otherwise, the victorious Stormcloaks will put [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane") in power.

Map of Whiterun Hold

Whiterun, the hold capital

## Topographical Overview

The hold borders six of the other eight [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), all but [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") and [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

Whiterun Hold is mostly covered in tundra and bordered by two major rivers (the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") to the south and the [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal") to the north), which makes the land fertile and well suited to farming.

### Flora and Fauna

The tundra is home to all manner of [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures"), from the large ([giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth")) to the small ([foxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox "Skyrim:Fox") and [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat")). The White River, flowing down from [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), is home to a large population of [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)").

The tundra is rich in [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly "Skyrim:Butterfly"). At night the butterflies are replaced by [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth"). Another location of interest is [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), where the pine forest stretching up from Falkreath Hold takes by. Here are forest plants like [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") and [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") more common than on the tundra. All types of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower"), except the yellow variant, can be found throughout the hold. The frail [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") variant however seems to thrive best around the rivers by Whiterun. The snowy parts, like [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), are only home to the humble [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries").

### Routes and Pathways

As the central hold in Skyrim, its main roads are in good condition, but a few of the more remote roads are not as well maintained. There are main roads heading southward to [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") through Riverwood and [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), eastward into [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") and [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), northward to [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), and westward to [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") through Rorikstead and to [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). Travelers should be encouraged to see that the main roads are regularly patrolled by [Whiterun Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard").

## Places

All locations in Whiterun Hold with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for their significance.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")** — A major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun)
-  **[Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach")** — The residence of the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Whiterun Hold, the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
- **[Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr")** — The mead hall headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jorrvaskr)
-  **[Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables")** — A [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") just outside the gates of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stables)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Bleakwind Basin](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Basin "Skyrim:Bleakwind Basin")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakwind+Basin)
-  **[Guldun Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Guldun_Rock "Skyrim:Guldun Rock")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guldun+Rock)
-  **[Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp")** — A small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") north of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halted+Stream+Camp)
-  **[Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt")** — A small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and ruin southwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Serpent%27s+Bluff+Redoubt)
-  **[Sleeping Tree Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Camp "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Camp")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sleeping+Tree+Camp)
-  **[Whiterun Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in Whiterun Hold, located east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") and far west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Whiterun Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Military Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") set up east of [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm") for the [attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") on [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Military+Camp)
-  **[Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in Whiterun Hold, located south of the [Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") and east of [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stormcloak+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
-  **[Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Fang+Cave)
-  **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through a mountain south-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
-  **[Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkshade)
-  **[Graywinter Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Graywinter_Watch "Skyrim:Graywinter Watch")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Graywinter+Watch)
-  **[Redoran's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west-northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redoran%27s+Retreat)
-  **[Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shimmermist+Cave)
-  **[South Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:South Cold Rock Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through a mountain south-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
-  **[Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Swindler%27s+Den)
-  **[White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River+Watch)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

-  **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
-  **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through a mountain south-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
-  **[Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument")** — A stone monument commemorating an ancient battle southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gjukar%27s+Monument)
-  **[Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow")** — A shallow outdoor cave west-northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greenspring+Hollow)
-  **[Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World")** — The highest mountain in Tamriel, located southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Throat+of+the+World)
- **[White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River")** — The longest river in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)"), stretching from the south of the province to the northeast corner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic

-  **[Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dustman%27s+Cairn)[†](#intnote_1)
-  **[Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest")** — A small outdoor graveyard and [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and a [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hamvir%27s+Rest)
-  **[Moldering Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moldering_Ruins "Skyrim:Moldering Ruins")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small [camp and concealed cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") west of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moldering+Ruins+%28DG%29)
-  **[Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east-northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [subjugated ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Subjugated_Ghost "Skyrim:Subjugated Ghost") and [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rannveig%27s+Fast)
-  **[Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silent+Moons+Camp)

[†](#note_1)Technically located in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach").

### Skyrim:Settlements including Farms , Orc Strongholds , and Inns

-  **[Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm")** — A farm just outside [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), owned by the [Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born "Skyrim:Battle-Born") clan who are influential in the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Battle-Born+Farm)
-  **[Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm")** — A small farm just outside of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), owned by [Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Chillfurrow+Farm)
-  **[Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage")** — An isolated [cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") at the foot of a mountain in northern Whiterun Hold, and south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Drelas%27+Cottage)
-  **[Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming") — An abandoned [farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Farms "Skyrim:Farms") east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenhills+Plantation+%28CC%29)
-  **[High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar")** — A small [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") roughly halfway up the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Hrothgar)
-  **[Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery")** — A small [meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") owned by [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Honningbrew+Meadery)
-  **[Lund's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Lund%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Lund's Hut")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lund%27s+Hut)
-  **[Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm")** — A large farm south of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") owned by [Severio Pelagia](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pelagia+Farm)
-  **[Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood")** — A lumber milling [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in southern Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riverwood)
-  **[Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead")** — A farming [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in western Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rorikstead)
-  **[Tundra Homestead](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead_(place) "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead") — A cottage that can be purchased in Whiterun Hold, located just northeast of [Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tundra+Homestead+%28CC%29)

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

-  **[The Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim, located east of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Ritual+Stone)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), and the mages' leader, [the Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fellglow+Keep)
-  **[Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Greymoor)
-  **[Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined [Nordic towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valtheim+Towers)
-  **[Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Western+Watchtower)
-  **[Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower")** — A small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whitewatch+Tower)

### Unmarked Places

- There are four [Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") in Whiterun Hold.
  - North of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave").
  - East of [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den").
  - Northwest of [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto").
  - West of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").
- There are four [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") in Whiterun Hold.
  - A [Shrine of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrine of Stendarr") south of [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den").
  - A [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") southeast of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave").
  - A [Shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrines") west of [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den").
  - A [Shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrines") north of [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave").
- Southeast of [Sleeping Tree Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Camp "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Camp") are three Stone Totems which unlock a gate with a skeleton and a chest.

## Whiterun Hold Quests

Quests that are started in or related to Whiterun Hold (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.
- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").
- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
- **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
- **[The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")**: Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane")**: Exploit the Time-Wound to learn [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") and defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") at the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World").
- **[The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen")**: Capture and interrogate [an ally](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").
- **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
- **[The World-Eater's Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:The_World-Eater%27s_Eyrie "Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie")**: Battle through [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn") to reach [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s portal to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").

### Imperial Legion Civil War Quests

- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Protect [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") from the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") invasion. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### College of Winterhold Quests

- **[Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books")**: Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").
- **[Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell")**: Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.

### Companions Quests

- **[Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms")**: Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
- **[Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor")**: Claim a [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") from [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn").
- **[The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand")**: Join the ranks of [the Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") and clear [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") of werewolf hunters.
- **[Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor")**: Claim the head of a [Glenmoril Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") for [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").
- **[Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")**: Retrieve the Fragments of Wuuthrad and wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

### Daedric and Divine Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").
- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

### Dark Brotherhood Quests

- **[Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial")**: Convince an unwilling [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius") to help fix a stranded [jester's](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") broken wagon wheel.
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.
- **[Kill Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Anoriath "Skyrim:Kill Anoriath")**: Kill [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Take the Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_the_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Take the Hidden Treasure")**: Torture the Brotherhood's prisoners for treasure.
- **[Locate the Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old")**: Find the Dark Brotherhood [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").

### Thieves Guild Quests

- **[Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits")**: Put [Maven Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") competition out of business.
- **[Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty")**: Help get a convicted prisoner released from jail.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Side Quests

- **[Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship")**: Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his [aunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his [ancestral barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").
- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").
- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

### Creation Club Quests

- **[Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put a stop to two bandit gangs wielding strange otherworldly equipment.
- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.
- **[The Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:The Staff of Hasedoki")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki"): Locate a legendary staff that's been smuggled into Skyrim.

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests are located in Whiterun Hold. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

## Bugs

- Although [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") are respectively located in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") and [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), crimes committed in either location may earn you a bounty here instead. **?**
- Shooting arrows at the carriage horse at your *Hearthfire* house may you earn a bounty here, regardless of whichever Hold you are in. **?**

Whiterun Imperial Camp

**Whiterun Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), located east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") and far west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

A bugged Legate Cipius, alone in the wilderness where the camp should be

The commanding officer of this camp is [Legate Quentin Cipius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Quentin_Cipius "Skyrim:Legate Quentin Cipius"). Unlike other military camps, you will never be welcome here, as it will only exist if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have taken [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in battle, by which time the player has irreversibly sided with the Stormcloaks. The soldiers will draw their [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and tell you to leave when you approach the camp. If you linger for too long, they will attack you. Like similar Imperial camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has neither a [quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster") or any [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Quentin Cipius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Quentin_Cipius "Skyrim:Legate Quentin Cipius") (commander)  [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") |

## Whiterun Imperial Camp

There are six soldiers in addition to the Legate and wounded. They are all armed with [imperial bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow") and [swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"), and all wear complete sets of [imperial light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"). The camp is situated around a central campfire on the banks of a shallow pond. There is a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") over the campfire, with an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside the fire. To the north is the command tent, containing an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of his time. There is a row of three small tents to the right of the command tent, each containing a bedroll. South of these tents is the Legate's tent, containing an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. To the right of the tent is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and farther to the right is a hospital tent, containing three bedrolls occupied by wounded soldiers and a low table holding two random potions of healing. Outside to the right is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and behind the table are some barrels.

## Notes

- There is a [shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar") east of the camp.
- Two ore veins are near the camp: a [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein east-northeast of the camp, and an [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") vein south-southwest of the camp.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

## Bugs

- At the very beginning of the game, Quentin Cipius spawns where the camp is supposed to be, standing in the wilderness. If you join the Stormcloaks and take over Whiterun, the camp will be set up, and Quentin will find a purpose in the wilderness. However, if you side with the Imperials and defend Whiterun, Quentin will show up in Dragonsreach, and the camp will never be built. Oddly, a duplicate of Quentin will still exist in the wilderness, even if Quentin is in Dragonsreach.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.

Whiterun Military Camp

**Whiterun Military Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") set up east of [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm") for the [attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") on [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

The camp only appears during the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"). The camp itself will appear regardless of the side you've chosen in the war, but a map marker will only be added during the Stormcloak version of the quest, in which case it immediately appears as discovered, allowing you to fast travel to the camp straight away.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q)  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Whiterun Military Camp

As soon as you arrive during the quest, the camp is in an uproar, with three catapults each manned by a Stormcloak soldier firing flaming missiles at Whiterun. The camp features a total of seven small tents, which contain no bed rolls or hay piles. In the middle of the camp is the command tent, containing a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side, with a [Stormcloak soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") studying the map. A few steps southeast of the command tent is a [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein. To the west of the main camp, [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") is giving a motivational speech to a group of ten Stormcloak soldiers.

## Notes

- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

## Bugs

- After the Battle for Whiterun, the camp's marker will be removed from the world map, but the camp itself won't be disbanded. It will instead remain even if the Empire wins the battle, along with a single, non-hostile Stormcloak soldier inside the main tent.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.10, fixes this bug.
-  Even after you complete the quest for the Stormcloaks, the Whiterun and Dragonsreach map markers will still be gone, and the Whiterun Military Camp marker will remain on the map. **?**
  - Entering Whiterun fixes this.

Before the completion of any related quests, there are 73 people in Whiterun (74 with the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on).

\* Only appears after [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising").
\*\* Only appears after the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").
\*\*\* Only appears after the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") quest [Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)").
\*\*\*\* Owns [Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm") but sleeps here.
† This person only sells goods at the market.

†† Backup innkeeper for [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda"); also backup merchant for [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor").

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

Whiterun Stables

**Whiterun Stables** is a [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") just outside the gates of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

Whiterun Stables is owned by [Lillith Maiden-Loom](/wiki/Skyrim:Lillith_Maiden-Loom "Skyrim:Lillith Maiden-Loom") and operated by [Skulvar Sable-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Skulvar_Sable-Hilt "Skyrim:Skulvar Sable-Hilt"), who also lives here with his son [Jervar](/wiki/Skyrim:Jervar "Skyrim:Jervar"). You can buy a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") from Skulvar for 1000 gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Horse Whisperer](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Whisperer "Skyrim:Horse Whisperer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Jervar](/wiki/Skyrim:Jervar "Skyrim:Jervar")  [Lillith Maiden-Loom](/wiki/Skyrim:Lillith_Maiden-Loom "Skyrim:Lillith Maiden-Loom")  [Skulvar Sable-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Skulvar_Sable-Hilt "Skyrim:Skulvar Sable-Hilt") [Hostler](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Hostler") |

## Exterior

The stables are to the right of the residence and consist of four stalls, two of which have gates on the front and always contain at least one [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). There are many food barrels in and around the stable and residence and a couple of [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") along the fence line. It is possible for both [Skulvar Sable-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Skulvar_Sable-Hilt "Skyrim:Skulvar Sable-Hilt") and his son [Jervar](/wiki/Skyrim:Jervar "Skyrim:Jervar") to die (see [bugs](#Bugs)). A carriage waits nearby driven by [Bjorlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjorlam "Skyrim:Bjorlam"), while beside this, once you have completed [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature") quest you will find [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") and her [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog").

| Plants | Animals |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 1 [Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") |

## Whiterun Stables

Inside the Whiterun Stables residence

The entrance to the stable residence is normally novice-locked, which can be opened using a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Key to Whiterun Stables") carried by [Skulvar Sable-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Skulvar_Sable-Hilt "Skyrim:Skulvar Sable-Hilt"), [Lillith Maiden-Loom](/wiki/Skyrim:Lillith_Maiden-Loom "Skyrim:Lillith Maiden-Loom") and [Jervar](/wiki/Skyrim:Jervar "Skyrim:Jervar"). Entering leads into a large room with a firepit opposite and a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") to the right. There are two doorways off of this room, one to the right of the firepit in the northern corner and the other in the western corner of the room. On your right when entering is a round wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat"). To the left is a cupboard with a bowl containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a couple of pieces of cheese on the shelves and a bottle of wine and a food sack on top. Against the southwest wall is a long wooden table and bench with a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of wine, a cabbage, a bowl containing [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese on top of the table. Hanging from the rafter above are four [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids and three whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)").

To the right of the table is the first doorway into a bedroom containing an owned bed in the southern corner with an end table to the left and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on the floor at the foot of the bed. On the end table is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), while in front, on the floor are a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). Against the northwest wall is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a bottle of wine, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on top. To the right of the firepit is a pair of wall shelves holding mainly clutter, but with a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") on a plate. By these is the second doorway into another bedroom used by Lillith. There is a single bed in the western corner with an end table to the left and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed. On the end table is a bowl containing four bottles of Nord mead and the chest contains only minor loot. Against the northwest wall is a small set of shelves with a display case on top containing a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), beside this is a set of clothes and on the lower shelf is a level-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). Against the northeast wall is a long end table with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a bottle of Nord mead, an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and a common book on top.

## Notes

- A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is located north of the stables. Go to the main gate, look left, go up the stairs and follow the wall.
- Whiterun Stables is the only stable in the game which only has one horse; all others have a saddled one and a bareback one.
-  Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the barrels outside the building as owned by the stables.

## Bugs

- There is a common occurrence of a bug here, when [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") becomes duplicated multiple times and/or becomes embedded in the ground just outside Whiterun after finishing [his quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep").
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
  -  His duplicates can be dealt with using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"): click on the Letrush duplicate and type `kill` followed by `disable`.
- There aren't enough beds for all of the people who live here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- If [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") and her dog reach the stables after you decide to repair the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") in [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature"), they'll stay here 24 hours a day.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Lilith Maiden-Loom can tell you to visit the stables to see the horses even if you're already here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Whiterun Stormcloak Camp

**Whiterun Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), located south of the [Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") and east of [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch").

Whiterun Stormcloak Camp

The camp is commanded by [Hjornskar Head-Smasher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjornskar_Head-Smasher "Skyrim:Hjornskar Head-Smasher"), and is never commanded by [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), as he commands the [Whiterun Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Military Camp") during the related quest. Unlike most Stormcloak camps, it has no [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Hjornskar Head-Smasher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjornskar_Head-Smasher "Skyrim:Hjornskar Head-Smasher") (commander)  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") |

## Related Quests

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Whiterun Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. To the northwest and southeast of the campfire are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. To the southwest of the campfire is the command tent, containing a lit brazier and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of his time. To the right of the command tent are some barrels. To the left of the command tent is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. To the east is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers. To the left of the hospital tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Behind the hospital tent are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. North of the campfire is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). Beyond the block beside a square stone arch is a workstation, consisting of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table and a crate hold various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). West of the workstation among some rubble is a locked chest.

Any time [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present; a hunter's camp will be here instead. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents.

## Bugs

- The camp may never be disabled after [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") is finished for the Stormcloaks.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

Whiterun

**Whiterun** is a major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). Its central location makes it the province's major commercial hub, as well as a crucial strategic point in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") between the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") loyalists and [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebels, as control of Whiterun Hold grants access to all surrounding lands. Whiterun is initially nominally aligned with the Empire, but [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") seems to care more about the people of Whiterun than either side of the conflict, rendering the hold effectively neutral.

Whiterun comprises three districts arranged in tiers and connected by stairways. The Plains District is the lowest and contains the city's marketplace and shops, inns, a few homes, and the city gates. The Wind District is the main residential area; it features the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), the ancient mead hall and headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), and the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge"), worked by the greatest blacksmith in Skyrim, [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). The Cloud District is dominated by the government seat [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and its [dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon"), and is the highest point in Whiterun. Local businesses and services include the smithy and weapons shop [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"), the tavern and hunting supply store [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods"), the alchemy shop [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), and [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") inn. The jarl's court wizard [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") has spells and enchanting supplies for sale and can teach you the basics of enchanting.

For more information on Whiterun, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Whiterun "Lore:Whiterun").

†† Backup innkeeper for [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda"); also backup merchant for [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor").

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

#### Main Quest

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of Whiterun about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near Whiterun.
- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

#### Companions

- See [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Quests "Skyrim:Companions").

#### Daedric

- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

#### Side Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

#### Creation Club

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.
- **[Smith 'N Slash](/wiki/Skyrim:Smith_%27N_Slash "Skyrim:Smith 'N Slash")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Defeat an [Orc blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and her bandits to obtain an enchanted set of armor.
- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.

| [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") | **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Bring one Mammoth Tusk to Ysolda |  |

## Notes

- [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). It may be purchased from [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") for 5,000 gold, as a reward for retrieving the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") for [Jarl Balgruuf's](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") court mage, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"). If it is not purchased at this point, and Whiterun is conquered by the Stormcloaks, it may be purchased from [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") as a reward for [helping the Stormcloaks conquer Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").
- Unused data in the game files indicates at least six buildings were removed from Whiterun: Maiden-Loom Manor, Pathway Guard Tower, Shrine of Talos, Ulfberth's House, Whiterun Jail, and Wintersand Manor.
- Approximately 220 alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") are freely available in Whiterun, with a respawn time of 30 days. These include 71 purple mountain flower, 41 blue mountain flower, 30 lavender, 23 tundra cotton, and 22 red mountain flower found throughout the city, as well as 14 nightshade in the graveyard outside the Hall of the Dead and 7 Nordic barnacle in the pool outside Dragonsreach.
- Whiterun also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Whiterun "Arena:Whiterun") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.
- There are 2 initial conversation scenes may be missed. [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith") and [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born")'s conversation, [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") and [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir")'s conversation only take place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- If you sprint as soon as you fast travel to Whiterun, the game may freeze.
- [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") may be found partially embedded into the ground just outside the city.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
- If you finish [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), the two [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") who started it will return to the city.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If the Stormcloaks take Whiterun, two guards will spawn on the left side of the main gate instead of one on either side.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Some of the items at the vendors in the marketplace aren't owned by them, allowing you to pick them up for free.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- A dialogue line referring to the Gildergreen here can be spoken by [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") in any city due to a missing condition check.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- You can leave the city without using the main gate by jumping on a barrel and over a wall near the gate. You can also do it by using the red plant formation on the north corner of House Gray-Mane.

Whiterun

**Whiterun** is a major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). Its central location makes it the province's major commercial hub, as well as a crucial strategic point in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") between the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") loyalists and [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebels, as control of Whiterun Hold grants access to all surrounding lands. Whiterun is initially nominally aligned with the Empire, but [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") seems to care more about the people of Whiterun than either side of the conflict, rendering the hold effectively neutral.

Whiterun comprises three districts arranged in tiers and connected by stairways. The Plains District is the lowest and contains the city's marketplace and shops, inns, a few homes, and the city gates. The Wind District is the main residential area; it features the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), the ancient mead hall and headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), and the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge"), worked by the greatest blacksmith in Skyrim, [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). The Cloud District is dominated by the government seat [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and its [dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon"), and is the highest point in Whiterun. Local businesses and services include the smithy and weapons shop [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"), the tavern and hunting supply store [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods"), the alchemy shop [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), and [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") inn. The jarl's court wizard [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") has spells and enchanting supplies for sale and can teach you the basics of enchanting.

For more information on Whiterun, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Whiterun "Lore:Whiterun").

#### Main Quest

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of Whiterun about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near Whiterun.
- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

#### Companions

- See [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Quests "Skyrim:Companions").

#### Daedric

- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

#### Side Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

#### Creation Club

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.
- **[Smith 'N Slash](/wiki/Skyrim:Smith_%27N_Slash "Skyrim:Smith 'N Slash")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Defeat an [Orc blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and her bandits to obtain an enchanted set of armor.
- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.

## Notes

- [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). It may be purchased from [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") for 5,000 gold, as a reward for retrieving the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") for [Jarl Balgruuf's](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") court mage, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"). If it is not purchased at this point, and Whiterun is conquered by the Stormcloaks, it may be purchased from [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") as a reward for [helping the Stormcloaks conquer Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").
- Unused data in the game files indicates at least six buildings were removed from Whiterun: Maiden-Loom Manor, Pathway Guard Tower, Shrine of Talos, Ulfberth's House, Whiterun Jail, and Wintersand Manor.
- Approximately 220 alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") are freely available in Whiterun, with a respawn time of 30 days. These include 71 purple mountain flower, 41 blue mountain flower, 30 lavender, 23 tundra cotton, and 22 red mountain flower found throughout the city, as well as 14 nightshade in the graveyard outside the Hall of the Dead and 7 Nordic barnacle in the pool outside Dragonsreach.
- Whiterun also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Whiterun "Arena:Whiterun") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.
- There are 2 initial conversation scenes may be missed. [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith") and [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born")'s conversation, [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") and [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir")'s conversation only take place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- If you sprint as soon as you fast travel to Whiterun, the game may freeze.
- [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") may be found partially embedded into the ground just outside the city.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
- If you finish [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), the two [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") who started it will return to the city.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If the Stormcloaks take Whiterun, two guards will spawn on the left side of the main gate instead of one on either side.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Some of the items at the vendors in the marketplace aren't owned by them, allowing you to pick them up for free.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- A dialogue line referring to the Gildergreen here can be spoken by [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") in any city due to a missing condition check.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- You can leave the city without using the main gate by jumping on a barrel and over a wall near the gate. You can also do it by using the red plant formation on the north corner of House Gray-Mane.

# Skyrim:Whiterun

## Overview

This article is about the city. For the hold, see [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").
