Whiterun

**Whiterun** is a major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). Its central location makes it the province's major commercial hub, as well as a crucial strategic point in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") between the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") loyalists and [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebels, as control of Whiterun Hold grants access to all surrounding lands. Whiterun is initially nominally aligned with the Empire, but [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") seems to care more about the people of Whiterun than either side of the conflict, rendering the hold effectively neutral.

Whiterun comprises three districts arranged in tiers and connected by stairways. The Plains District is the lowest and contains the city's marketplace and shops, inns, a few homes, and the city gates. The Wind District is the main residential area; it features the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), the ancient mead hall and headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), and the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge"), worked by the greatest blacksmith in Skyrim, [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). The Cloud District is dominated by the government seat [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and its [dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon"), and is the highest point in Whiterun. Local businesses and services include the smithy and weapons shop [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"), the tavern and hunting supply store [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods"), the alchemy shop [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), and [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") inn. The jarl's court wizard [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") has spells and enchanting supplies for sale and can teach you the basics of enchanting.

For more information on Whiterun, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Whiterun "Lore:Whiterun").

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

#### Main Quest

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of Whiterun about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near Whiterun.
- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

#### Companions

- See [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Quests "Skyrim:Companions").

#### Daedric

- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

#### Side Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

#### Creation Club

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.
- **[Smith 'N Slash](/wiki/Skyrim:Smith_%27N_Slash "Skyrim:Smith 'N Slash")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Defeat an [Orc blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and her bandits to obtain an enchanted set of armor.
- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.

## Notes

- [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). It may be purchased from [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") for 5,000 gold, as a reward for retrieving the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") for [Jarl Balgruuf's](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") court mage, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"). If it is not purchased at this point, and Whiterun is conquered by the Stormcloaks, it may be purchased from [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") as a reward for [helping the Stormcloaks conquer Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").
- Unused data in the game files indicates at least six buildings were removed from Whiterun: Maiden-Loom Manor, Pathway Guard Tower, Shrine of Talos, Ulfberth's House, Whiterun Jail, and Wintersand Manor.
- Approximately 220 alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") are freely available in Whiterun, with a respawn time of 30 days. These include 71 purple mountain flower, 41 blue mountain flower, 30 lavender, 23 tundra cotton, and 22 red mountain flower found throughout the city, as well as 14 nightshade in the graveyard outside the Hall of the Dead and 7 Nordic barnacle in the pool outside Dragonsreach.
- Whiterun also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Whiterun "Arena:Whiterun") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.
- There are 2 initial conversation scenes may be missed. [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith") and [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born")'s conversation, [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") and [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir")'s conversation only take place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- If you sprint as soon as you fast travel to Whiterun, the game may freeze.
- [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") may be found partially embedded into the ground just outside the city.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
- If you finish [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), the two [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") who started it will return to the city.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If the Stormcloaks take Whiterun, two guards will spawn on the left side of the main gate instead of one on either side.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Some of the items at the vendors in the marketplace aren't owned by them, allowing you to pick them up for free.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- A dialogue line referring to the Gildergreen here can be spoken by [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") in any city due to a missing condition check.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- You can leave the city without using the main gate by jumping on a barrel and over a wall near the gate. You can also do it by using the red plant formation on the north corner of House Gray-Mane.

# Skyrim:Whiterun

## Overview

This article is about the city. For the hold, see [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").

Whiterun

**Whiterun** is a major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). Its central location makes it the province's major commercial hub, as well as a crucial strategic point in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") between the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") loyalists and [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebels, as control of Whiterun Hold grants access to all surrounding lands. Whiterun is initially nominally aligned with the Empire, but [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") seems to care more about the people of Whiterun than either side of the conflict, rendering the hold effectively neutral.

Whiterun comprises three districts arranged in tiers and connected by stairways. The Plains District is the lowest and contains the city's marketplace and shops, inns, a few homes, and the city gates. The Wind District is the main residential area; it features the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), the ancient mead hall and headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), and the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge"), worked by the greatest blacksmith in Skyrim, [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). The Cloud District is dominated by the government seat [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and its [dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon"), and is the highest point in Whiterun. Local businesses and services include the smithy and weapons shop [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"), the tavern and hunting supply store [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods"), the alchemy shop [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), and [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") inn. The jarl's court wizard [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") has spells and enchanting supplies for sale and can teach you the basics of enchanting.

For more information on Whiterun, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Whiterun "Lore:Whiterun").

\*\*\*\* Owns [Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm") but sleeps here.
† This person only sells goods at the market.

†† Backup innkeeper for [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda"); also backup merchant for [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor").

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

#### Main Quest

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of Whiterun about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near Whiterun.
- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

#### Companions

- See [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Quests "Skyrim:Companions").

#### Daedric

- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

#### Side Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

#### Creation Club

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.
- **[Smith 'N Slash](/wiki/Skyrim:Smith_%27N_Slash "Skyrim:Smith 'N Slash")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Defeat an [Orc blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and her bandits to obtain an enchanted set of armor.
- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.

## Notes

- [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). It may be purchased from [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") for 5,000 gold, as a reward for retrieving the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") for [Jarl Balgruuf's](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") court mage, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"). If it is not purchased at this point, and Whiterun is conquered by the Stormcloaks, it may be purchased from [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") as a reward for [helping the Stormcloaks conquer Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").
- Unused data in the game files indicates at least six buildings were removed from Whiterun: Maiden-Loom Manor, Pathway Guard Tower, Shrine of Talos, Ulfberth's House, Whiterun Jail, and Wintersand Manor.
- Approximately 220 alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") are freely available in Whiterun, with a respawn time of 30 days. These include 71 purple mountain flower, 41 blue mountain flower, 30 lavender, 23 tundra cotton, and 22 red mountain flower found throughout the city, as well as 14 nightshade in the graveyard outside the Hall of the Dead and 7 Nordic barnacle in the pool outside Dragonsreach.
- Whiterun also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Whiterun "Arena:Whiterun") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.
- There are 2 initial conversation scenes may be missed. [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith") and [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born")'s conversation, [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") and [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir")'s conversation only take place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- If you sprint as soon as you fast travel to Whiterun, the game may freeze.
- [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") may be found partially embedded into the ground just outside the city.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
- If you finish [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), the two [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") who started it will return to the city.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If the Stormcloaks take Whiterun, two guards will spawn on the left side of the main gate instead of one on either side.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Some of the items at the vendors in the marketplace aren't owned by them, allowing you to pick them up for free.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- A dialogue line referring to the Gildergreen here can be spoken by [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") in any city due to a missing condition check.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- You can leave the city without using the main gate by jumping on a barrel and over a wall near the gate. You can also do it by using the red plant formation on the north corner of House Gray-Mane.

# Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Imperial Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Imperial_Tower.png) | Imperial Tower: Whitewatch Tower ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whitewatch+Tower)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WhitewatchTowerExterior01 | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |
| Location | |
| North-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") South of [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Whitewatch Tower

**Whitewatch Tower** is a small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

## Walkthrough

Depending on the faction that currently controls Whiterun, the tower is occupied by either [Whiterun guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") or [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier"). The structure comprises a largely intact eastern watchtower and a ruined western tower connected by an archway. The tower is flanked with yellow Whiterun banners if the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") has control, or blue Stormcloak banners if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have control. [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") grow near the entrance. Passing under the arch into the courtyard, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is on the south side of the eastern tower near a stone wall. Some meager provisions for the guards are near the arch, while a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") among the crates holds more substantial treasure. More lavender grows in the courtyard. A weapon rack to the south holds two [Imperial swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") if the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") occupy the tower, or an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), and a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") are in control. Wooden ramps lead up to the eastern tower, which features nothing of interest. However, jumping onto the ledge on the west side of the tower behind the guard's chair and crossing over the archway leads you to the ruined western tower, where an apprentice-locked chest is buried in the rubble.

## Notes

- [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") may attack the tower as you approach.
- Caution is advised when unlocking the chests around the tower; if the guards see you, you will receive a bounty.
- If you unlock the apprentice-level chest buried in the rubble, you may not get a bounty.
- If the leveled sword next to the Imperial swords is an iron or steel sword, you can take it without penalty.
- A leveled strongbox is to the northwest between some stone blocks on the top of a hill.
- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") are 250 feet south of the tower at the base of the [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") hill.
- A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") is 400 feet south of the tower up the hill. Just east of the vein is a novice-locked chest.
- An [unmarked bandit camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Whiterun#Smuggler.27s_Den:_Whiterun "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Whiterun") is southwest of the tower under a cliff at the base of the Dragonsreach hill. It is occupied by leveled bandits and features a wide variety of loot, including alchemical ingredients, weapons, potions, and the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Aevar Stone-Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Aevar_Stone-Singer "Skyrim:Aevar Stone-Singer")*. The [Smugglers' Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Smugglers%27_Note "Skyrim:Smugglers' Note") can also be found under a table in the camp. A [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") and a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") can be found here as well, although the horse must be stolen to be ridden.

## Bugs

- The Imperial swords and the leveled sword may be hovering in the air in front of their respective weapon racks. **?**
- The guards stationed here use the line "Be glad you're here in the city, and not out in Riverwood. Those poor sods don't even have a wall." This line indicates the tower is in the city of Whiterun itself, when it clearly isn't.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.4, addresses this issue. The "Be glad you're here in the city, and not out in Riverwood. Those poor sods don't even have a wall." line has been removed from the guards stationed at the tower.

Widow's Watch Ruins

**Widow's Watch Ruins** is a small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") west-northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing a [hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag").

## Walkthrough

This is a typical tower that has tilted due to a landslide, making traversal slightly difficult. Once you have defeated the lone hag, you are free to explore. Keep climbing the structure to the top, then loop around counterclockwise until you reach a higher doorway. Through the doorway, ascend the wooden stairs and cross the wooden plank to reach an expert-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") partially hidden behind a table, next to which is a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Rain's Hand, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Rain%27s_Hand,_v4 "Skyrim:2920, Rain's Hand, v4")* behind a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). There is nothing else of interest here.

## Notes

- Sometimes the book and shield can be dislodged and found elsewhere around the tower and surrounding area.
- Widow's Watch Ruins also appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Sword's Point Watchtower](/wiki/Online:Sword%27s_Point_Watchtower "Online:Sword's Point Watchtower").
- Version 2.0.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the Imperial tower map icon for Widow's Watch Ruins with the one for Nordic towers.

## Bugs

- This location cannot be cleared, as it lacks the proper location keywords to do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17666))

# Skyrim:Wind and Sand (quest)

## Overview

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Destruction 40 | | ← Previous | [Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends") and [Experimental Subject](/wiki/Skyrim:Experimental_Subject "Skyrim:Experimental Subject") | | |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") about assisting him in his research.
2. Go to a radiant location and retrieve *[Wind and Sand](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_and_Sand_(book) "Skyrim:Wind and Sand (book)")*.
3. Return to Neloth for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After completing [Experimental Subject](/wiki/Skyrim:Experimental_Subject "Skyrim:Experimental Subject"), speak to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") again about assisting in his research. This time, he will tell you that he is attempting to adapt Redguard magic to the island's ash. He has learned the location of a book through a source of his that would prove invaluable to his spell research. The book is *[Wind and Sand](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_and_Sand_(book) "Skyrim:Wind and Sand (book)")* and is located in a radiant location: a Dragon lair, dragon priest lair, draugr crypt, Falmer hive, Forsworn camp, hagraven nest, vampire lair, or warlock lair.

Once you have the book, return to Neloth who will excitedly declare that he can create some sort of wind spell with its contents. You will receive 250 gold, and the spell tome [Whirlwind Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Cloak "Skyrim:Whirlwind Cloak") will be made available for purchase the next time that [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") restocks.

## Quest Stages

| Wind and Sand (DLC2TTR3b) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Neloth has asked me to get a copy Wind and Sand from inside <Alias=Dungeon>. He needs it for his spell research. *Objective 100:* Get the Wind and Sand book |
| 200 |  | I found a copy of Wind and Sand from inside <alias=dungeon>. Neloth needs it for his spell research. *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 | ☑ | I found a copy of Wind and Sand from inside <alias=dungeon>. Neloth needed it for his spell research. I should be able to buy the spell from Talvas. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR3b stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR3b`.

# Skyrim:Wind Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Standing Stones.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Standing_Stones.png) | All-Maker Stone: Wind Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Wind+Stone)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2StoneWind | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| West-northwest of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") North-northeast of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") | |

The Wind Stone

The **Wind Stone** is an [All-Maker Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones") west-northwest of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

Once [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), this stone gives you the power to cast an [area spell](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Wind "Skyrim:North Wind") that deals 20 points of frost damage for 10 seconds, plus stamina damage. Once you use this power, it disappears from the Powers menu, and you must return to the Wind Stone to obtain it again.

## Related Quests

- **[The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal")**: Find a way to free the citizens of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

## Walkthrough

Lurker attacking

The stone shows the usual signs of construction, with wooden scaffolding on the northwest side, and [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), [shovels](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel"), hammers, and carts in the vicinity. Several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants and [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes grow around the stone. A path leads south-southwest to the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") and the [Beast Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Stone "Skyrim:Beast Stone"), with a branching path leading east to Skaal Village.

Before you cleanse the stone, [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper"), [Deor Woodcutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter"), [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla"), [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice"), [Morwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen "Skyrim:Morwen"), [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan"), and [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood") will be working on and bowing to the stone. When you cleanse the stone, a leveled [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") will rise from the water around the base of the stone and attack you and the workers. After the lurker is defeated, the workers will express their thanks and return to Skaal Village.

## Dialogue

The citizens of Skaal Village will have the following dialogue after the stone is cleansed.

**Baldor**: *"I... I don't know how I got here."*
**Baldor**: *"Is this a dream? No, it is a nightmare, surely."*
**Deor**: *"A fever must have taken me. What else could explain this?"*
**Deor**: *"Thank you, my friend. You have set us free."*
**Edla**: *"This... this is some dark magic. It has to be."*
**Edla**: *"Who are you? What am I doing here?"*
**Fanari**: *"The whole village is here! What sorcery is this?"*
**Fanari**: *"All-Maker bless you! You have saved us!"*
**Morwen**: *"Why was I building a temple?"*
**Morwen**: *"I must be going mad. But then, so must everyone else."*
**Tharstan**: *"What in Mundus am I doing out here at this hour?"*
**Tharstan**: *"This is both fascinating and terrifying."*
**Wulf**: *"I pray to the All-Maker that whatever this was, it doesn't happen again."*
**Wulf**: *"I don't know what spell you freed us from, outsider, but I thank you."*

**Baldor**: *"I can't speak now, friend. I must return home."*
**Deor**: *"I don't mean to be rude outsider, but I must get back to the village."*
**Edla**: *"I have no time to speak now, outsider. I'm on my way home."*
**Fanari**: *"I must get back to the village. As leader of the Skaal, I'm needed there."*
**Morwen**: *"Sorry friend, but I'm on the road home. Find me there and perhaps we can talk."*
**Wulf**: *"My road takes me home, outsider. Hunt well."*

## Notes

- The Wind Stone also appears in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Wind_Stone "Bloodmoon:Wind Stone")*.

# Skyrim:Windhelm Military Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |

Windhelm Military Camp

**Windhelm Military Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") set up east of [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm") for the [attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") on [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

The camp only appears during the [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") in the Imperial Legion questline.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") |

## Related Quests

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

## Windhelm Military Camp

It features several small tents, which contain no bed rolls or hay piles. Several tree stumps are scattered in the area, with one near the central campfire being a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). In the middle of the camp is a table holding Imperial weapons, as well as an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). To the southeast past most of the tents is another campfire. Up the hill to the southwest is another small tent, a large empty tent, and the command tent, containing a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. In the western section of the camp, three catapults are aimed at Windhelm.

When this camp is not present, a hunter's camp will be here instead.

## Notes

- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map displays the hunter camp; the previous one displayed the military camp.

## Bugs

- After the Battle for Windhelm, the camp's marker will be removed from the world map, and the Imperial soldiers will be disabled, but the camp itself won't be disbanded.

# Skyrim:Windhelm Stables

## Overview

Windhelm Stables

**Windhelm Stables** is a [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") outside of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

You can purchase a bay [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") with white markings for 1000 gold from [Ulundil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulundil "Skyrim:Ulundil"). If Ulundil dies, his wife, [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya"), will instead offer to sell you the stables' horses. It consists of one area only, *[Windhelm Stables](#Windhelm_Stables)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Horse Whisperer](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Whisperer "Skyrim:Horse Whisperer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya")  [Ulundil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulundil "Skyrim:Ulundil") [Hostler](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Hostler") |

## Exterior

Two flights of stairs (one from the stony path leading to Windhelm, and one from the carriage) lead to a small stony yard in front of the house. There is a table outside the entrance door with a wine bottle on it. Between the table and the entrance are five food sacks on the ground (two large, two normal, and one small). Beneath the stairs connecting the house and stables is one bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") cooling in the snow, just out of the way, and some barrels behind. The stables hold some barrels, four food sacks (two large and two normal), a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") (without a woodcutter's axe, which is to be found inside the house, on the shelves just above the strongbox), two horses (of which one is saddled), and bales of straw. Outside the stables, along the road to [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm"), is a trough containing a bottle of wine next to a pile of firewood. Behind those, some crates are along the eastern wall.

| Animals | Other |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") | 1 [Wood Chopping Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") |

## Windhelm Stables

Inside Windhelm Stables

The stable building is one room only, with a double bed along the western wall. In the southwestern corner is a wardrobe with [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and in the opposite corner sits a dresser, also with clothes, and with the *[Business Ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger")* and a small coin purse on top. Two sets of shelves decorate the northern wall, and display a [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), some [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of Nord mead, a wheel of [eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), and two food sacks. Opposite the shelves, next to the front door, is a table with a few common books. The eastern part of the stable house is reserved for dining, and has four food sacks, three large and one small. The dinner table is placed in front of the roaring fireplace, which features a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit"). The table itself holds some assorted food, a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread").

## Notes

- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") moves the bottle of Nord mead outside the building so that it stands on the snow, rather than clipping through it.
  - It does, however, mark everything outside the building as owned by the stables.

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

[^b](#note_adelaisa)Only appears once you return from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") with information during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") for Orthus.

[^c](#note_brelasmalborn)Only present depending on choices made during the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest.

[^d](#note_ship)Provides initial transportation to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

[^e](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Windhelm

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

[^e](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

[^a](#note_market)Only sells goods at the market.

[^b](#note_adelaisa)Only appears once you return from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") with information during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") for Orthus.

[^c](#note_brelasmalborn)Only present depending on choices made during the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest.

[^d](#note_ship)Provides initial transportation to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

[^e](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
