Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

[^a](#note_market)Only sells goods at the market.

[^b](#note_adelaisa)Only appears once you return from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") with information during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") for Orthus.

[^c](#note_brelasmalborn)Only present depending on choices made during the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest.

[^d](#note_ship)Provides initial transportation to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

[^e](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

| - [Clan Shatter-Shield Office](/wiki/Skyrim:Clan_Shatter-Shield_Office "Skyrim:Clan Shatter-Shield Office") - [East Empire Company](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_(place) "Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)") - [Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Warehouse "Skyrim:Warehouse") |

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Windhelm

**Windhelm** is a major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Lying near the coast at the northern tip of Eastmarch, the city is extremely cold and frequently experiences blizzards. The ruler of Windhelm is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the leader of the [Stormcloak Rebellion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), who resides in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). The city does not comply with the Imperial ban on [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worship and features a [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos"), and anti-foreign sentiment is common among the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population.

The temple and [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") lie along the main avenue of Windhelm, in the Stone Quarter. To the west is an open-air market, where [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") operates a general goods stall with a nearby [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") sells fresh meats, and [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") sells produce. The oldest section of the city is Valunstrad, "Avenue of Valor" in the old Nord language, which contains the palace and several residential buildings. Because of its proximity to Morrowind, Windhelm also hosts a sizable population of [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sought refuge in Skyrim after the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The Dark Elves are confined to a cramped slum below the rest of Windhelm called the Gray Quarter, previously known as the Snow Quarter. The Dunmer are not violently persecuted, but the local Nords are suspicious and outwardly xenophobic, while Ulfric Stormcloak turns a blind eye to their plight. [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") also populate Windhelm, but are prohibited from entering the city itself and are forced to live and work on the docks outside the walls. [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), a supporter of the Argonians and Dark Elves, believes the Argonians must remain outside the city for their own safety from the prejudiced Nords who follow Ulfric's beliefs.

For more information on Windhelm, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Windhelm "Lore:Windhelm").

[^a](#note_market)Only sells goods at the market.

[^b](#note_adelaisa)Only appears once you return from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") with information during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") for Orthus.

[^c](#note_brelasmalborn)Only present depending on choices made during the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest.

[^d](#note_ship)Provides initial transportation to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

[^e](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.

#### Side Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: Windhelm is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in Windhelm.

| Windhelm not [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") | [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") | **[Delivery (Hillevi)](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Hillevi) "Skyrim:Delivery (Hillevi)")**: Deliver a bottle of [Nightshade Extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade_Extact "Skyrim:Nightshade Extact") to [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving"). | - Deliver the Nightshade Extact *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* to Wuunferth the Unliving |  |

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capital and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

#### Creation Club

- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Notes

- Although the name "Valunstrad" does not appear in the game, the northwest district of the city (including the palace, barracks, and mansions north of the market) is named this in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.
- [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests related to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 to 12,000 gold.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Windhelm Docks.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the everything in docks as owned, regardless whether they were owned originally or not.
- Windhelm also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Windhelm "Arena:Windhelm")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Windhelm "Online:Windhelm").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") and [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s conversation only takes place between 8am~8pm, and if the player never enters the related area.

## Bugs

- Some of the walls in Windhelm will spurt blood when hit with a weapon.
- One of the barrels on the docks may clip with barrels stacked below it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Windpeak Inn

**Windpeak Inn** is an inn in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). It is the first place you'll pass coming off the road into Dawnstar. [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring") runs the inn, rents rooms, and sells typical innkeeper merchandise ([food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Beverages "Skyrim:Beverages")). His daughter, [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(bard) "Skyrim:Karita (bard)"), is the inn's bard, and takes over renting rooms and selling food and drinks if her father dies. [Abelone](/wiki/Skyrim:Abelone "Skyrim:Abelone") and [Erandur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur") also live here. Erandur only lives here until you start the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") and you agree to accompany him.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Abelone](/wiki/Skyrim:Abelone "Skyrim:Abelone")  [Erandur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(bard) "Skyrim:Karita (bard)") ([Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances")) [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") \*  [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring") (Owner) [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Alesan](/wiki/Skyrim:Alesan "Skyrim:Alesan") [HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")\*\*  [Vereth](/wiki/Skyrim:Vereth "Skyrim:Vereth") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set")\*\*\* |

\* This person only becomes innkeeper if Thoring is dead.

## Related Quests

- **[Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare")**: Relieve the people of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") from [Vaermina](/wiki/Lore:Vaermina "Lore:Vaermina")'s curse.
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set"): Investigate the mysterious disappearances of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

### Exterior

There are two sets of steps leading up to the partially covered porch; to the left of the main set are two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and two food barrels. To the right of the building there is a small farm plot with a small lean-to housing a chicken's nest that contains a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") next to a long wooden table with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top. Also, just beyond the fence there is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block").

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 2 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 1 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Windpeak Inn

Windpeak inn

When you first enter the place Karita, [Fruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Fruki "Skyrim:Fruki") and [Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir") are having a conversation about the nightmares occurring in Dawnstar, while Erandur tries to explain things and calm them down. You enter into the main common room with a central firepit and five long wooden benches, two against the north wall and three against the south. Four of the table hold several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a couple of bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") or [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") or both. The end table against the south wall also has two chicken's eggs on it and the table on your right, against the north wall has a selection of cheese pieces and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on it. Along the west wall are several barrels and a pile of firewood. Against this wall is normally where [Alesan](/wiki/Skyrim:Alesan "Skyrim:Alesan") sleeps on the floor.

At the eastern end of the room is a counter with several pieces of cheese, a bottle of wine and a bottle of alto wine on top. Under the counter are fourteen bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), six bottles of wine, two bottles of alto wine, a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), three small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Along the wall behind the counter are a row of vats and several barrels of foodstuffs. There are three hanging racks holding ten [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") as well as two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") all hanging from the ceiling.

There are two doorways to bedrooms on the north wall and one on the south wall that is much larger. The one on the south wall is the room you are shown to if you rent a room. It contains a single bed in the southeast corner, against the east wall. To the right of this are two dressers containing [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"). The dresser on the left holds two bottles of alto wine, a [tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard"), a lit candle, and a copy of [The Cabin in the Woods](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cabin_in_the_Woods "Skyrim:The Cabin in the Woods"). Between both dressers is a bucket holding a broom. Against the west wall are a pile of food sacks and a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Next to the north wall is a chair next to a square wooden table holding a lit candle, a tankard, a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), and a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). There are three [baskets](/wiki/Skyrim:Basket "Skyrim:Basket") between the chest and the chair, and one more just to the right of the square table. You can take everything from this room for free, except for the broom and bucket. On either side of the doorway to the large bedroom are two sets of shelves holding three bunches of elves ear, seven bottles of Nord mead, four loaves of bread, two bottles of alto wine and six bottles of wine. The set of shelves on the left side of the doorway also has a barrel next to it.

The left-hand bedroom on the north side consists of a single owned bed in the northwest corner, against the west wall, with a table and chair to the right of it. On the table is a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a copy of [Song of the Askelde Men](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Askelde_Men "Skyrim:Song of the Askelde Men"). At the foot of the bed is an unlocked chest and between this and the doorway is a wardrobe also against the west wall containing clothes. The right-hand bedroom is quite similar except the single owned bed is in the northeast corner and along the east wall, with an unlocked chest at the foot of the bed, but with a dresser containing clothes between this and the doorway. To the left of the bed is a table and chair. On the table is a copy of [A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde").

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the Windpeak Inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 7 | Random drinks |
| 10 | Random inn food |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"Windpeak Inn is Dawnstar's only tavern and is run by Thoring and his young daughter Karita, who both live in the building. Karita serves as a bard, and their servant Abelone handles most of the menial chores, chopping wood or using the grindstone in the pen outside. Currently, the place is a meeting spot where anxious townsfolk (such as Fruki and Irgnir the miners) gather to gossip and worry about the strange nightmares that have been keeping them from their beds."*

- You can find a wooden bowl and a tankard outside one of the guestroom walls, but you'll have to clip through it to gain access.

## Bugs

- Although Thoring is supposed to provide innkeeper merchant services, he was not added to the `ServicesDawnstarWindpeakInn` faction, nor was anyone else. Therefore it is not possible to purchase food and drink at this inn.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- NPCs standing between the bar stools will not be able to move.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.0, fixes this bug.
- After you finish "Rise in the East", [Stig Salt-Plank](/wiki/Skyrim:Stig_Salt-Plank "Skyrim:Stig Salt-Plank") and his men may permanently remain here, and only say general quotes if you talk to them. **?**

# Skyrim:Windstad Manor

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Town.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Town.png) | House: Windstad Manor ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windstad+Manor+%28HF%29)) | | |
| Added by | [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BYOHHouse2Exterior | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav")  South of [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Windstad Manor

**Windstad Manor** is a piece of property in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), north of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and east of the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack"). It is one of three potential homes available with the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on.

Aerial view of the house with the Alchemy, Enchanting, and Library additions

After installing Hearthfire, you may purchase this plot of land at [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). If [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") is still the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), speak with her [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward"), [Aslfur](/wiki/Skyrim:Aslfur "Skyrim:Aslfur"); if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have control of the hold, speak with the new jarl, [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") or her husband [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur"). You will have to complete the quest [Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest") before being allowed to purchase land if Idgrod is still jarl; Sorli will allow you to purchase it out of gratitude for your help installing her, whether that was because of [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or [conquering Hjaalmarch for the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)"). When you ask if you can buy a house in the hold, you will be told that there are no houses for sale at that time, but a new plot of land is available. It will cost 5,000 gold.

Your new property, Windstad Manor, will be marked as an undiscovered location on your map, located in the northern part of Hjaalmarch on a small hill, south of [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") and just east of where the land lowers into the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts").

When you arrive on your new plot of land, you will find a drafting table, carpenter's bench, [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and chest south of the housebuilding area, just before the treeline. A "[Log Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")" can be found slightly north of the drafting table. A [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit") is directly adjacent to the north end of the log pile, while a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is a short distance further north, embedded in the cliff wall on the east side just before two snow-laden trees. Directly west from this point, towards the water, is a second clay deposit; another stone quarry is in the cliff wall just behind it.

You can begin [building](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") your home immediately, with materials provided in the chest when you first arrive. A unique feature at Windstad Manor is you have the option to build a fish hatchery. Once built, the hatchery appears a distance north of your property, next to the second clay deposit previously mentioned. If you place any [fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish "Skyrim:Fish") or fish eggs ([Slaughterfish Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") or [Salmon Roe](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Roe "Skyrim:Salmon Roe")) in the column at the end of the jetty (only one of each species will be accepted) and return to your property in seven days, the netted area of water will contain several offspring of that fish. The [Slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") that spawn are tame and will not attack you. The house entrance will face to the south; looking west from there affords an impressive view of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") atop its natural arch.

Like the other player-built homes, you will have the option to expand onto your home with a [Main Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Hall "Skyrim:Main Hall"), cellar, and three wing additions. See [this page](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Furnishing_Options "Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Furnishing Options") for pages detailing the furnishing options in each part of your home.

Should you become a [Thane of Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch"), [Valdimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdimar "Skyrim:Valdimar") will become your [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"). He will move to Windstad Manor upon construction of the [small house](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_House_Layout "Skyrim:Small House Layout") layout.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Engar](/wiki/Skyrim:Engar "Skyrim:Engar")  [Sonir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sonir "Skyrim:Sonir")  [Valdimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdimar "Skyrim:Valdimar") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

## Related Quests

- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**: Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")**: [Construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") a house for yourself.
- **[Thane of Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Fish Hatchery

The Fish Hatchery

Multiple types of fish may be added at the same time to the hatchery and all will eventually mature. The following can be raised in the hatchery:

- [Abacean Longfin](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Abacean_Longfin "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")
- [Clam](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Clam "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") (using [Clam Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat"))
- [Cyrodilic Spadetail](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Cyrodilic_Spadetail "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")
- [Histcarp](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Histcarp "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")
- [River Betty](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#River_Betty "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")
- [Salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Salmon "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") (using [Salmon Roe](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Roe "Skyrim:Salmon Roe")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"))
  - Roe can be harvested after killing the salmon with the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout.
- [Silverside Perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")
- [Slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") (using [Slaughterfish Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"))
  - The offspring are not hostile to you, and slaughterfish egg nests will appear next to the jetty.

[Dragonflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonfly "Skyrim:Dragonfly") may appear above the water of the fishery as well. [Nordic Barnacle Clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle Cluster") and [Pearl Oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") cannot be bred in the hatchery even though they are aquatic creatures.

You can farm many different types of fish with the Hatchery, including those added by [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, all of the new fish can be added to the hatchery. The only exception is [Juvenile Mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Juvenile_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Juvenile Mudcrab")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"). It is not necessary to deposit an [Angler](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler "Skyrim:Angler")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") in the hatchery; placing a single [Angler Larvae](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Larvae "Skyrim:Angler Larvae")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") in the hatchery will result in respawning stocks of both larval and fully-grown anglers.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | - [Angelfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Angelfish "Skyrim:Angelfish")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") - [Angler Larvae](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Larvae "Skyrim:Angler Larvae")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") / [Angler](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler "Skyrim:Angler")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") - ## Notes

- There is a group of three [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") near the hatchery. They may become tame once the hatchery has been constructed (see [bugs](#Bugs)).
- Frequent [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") (dead and undead), [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"), and bandit spawns may occur here.
- One of the possible locations for a rupture to appear as part of [Aftershock](/wiki/Skyrim:Aftershock "Skyrim:Aftershock") is located just beside the house.
- While living in Windstad Manor, [adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") female children will sometimes say, *"This place is scary. There are monsters in the swamp, I just know it."*
  - For the reactions given by your spouse, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Spouse_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue").
- The [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") adds furnishings to your home each time you cross the property border. These borders include:
  - Go straight east from your entrance door, up the hill. The border is between the two trees growing next to the rocks on your left (there is a third tree on your right).
  - North of the house. Past the quarried stone deposit and smelter, there are two trees. The border is just between the trees.
- Original surface items do respawn after 10 consecutive days of the house not being visited.
- The nest on the roof of the Main Hall yields a Rock Warbler Egg rather than the Hawk's Egg spawned at the other two Hearthfire houses.
  - Version 3.0.11 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") replaces the Rock Warbler nest on the roof with a Hawk's nest.
- The fish hatchery can support Histcarp, Salmon, and Silverside Perch. The combination of Histcarp, Salmon Roe, and Silverside Perch is one of the most valuable in the game that uses only farmable ingredients. This combination is special in that it only needs the fish hatchery, no other farming resource
  - Angelfish, Juniper Berries, and Salmon Roe is the highest-value potion using only farmable ingredients. Angelfish, Garlic, and Salmon Roe is of equal value as Garlic, Nordic Barnacle, and Salmon Roe while using two farmable ingredients instead of one.
  - Without using the Fishing creation, other high-value potions combine Histcarp, Salmon Roe, and one of Creep Cluster, Jazbay Grapes, Juniper Berries, or Wheat.

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses. See the [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.
- You may not receive the [Windstad Manor Charter](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor_Charter "Skyrim:Windstad Manor Charter") after purchasing the plot.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
- When Valdimar is assigned as a Housecarl for this property, he may be found in [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") or [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor") instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes Sonir can get stuck in the fireplace if it is built.
- You may not be able to purchase the furnishings for the entryway after building it. Also, purchased furnishings for all other rooms may not appear.
- The option to purchase furnishings for the entryway may still be available after you have already bought them. If you try to select it a second time, your steward will refuse, acting as if you do not have enough gold to buy the furniture.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The workbench in the cellar may not be removeable with the drafting table.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.1, fixes this bug.
  -  To remove it, open the console, click on the table and type `disable`. You can place it again if you still have it selected in the console by typing `enable`, or by using the drafting table.
- The alchemy lab in the Alchemy Laboratory may not work properly.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- After purchasing the land and beginning construction, the house may not appear.
- After adding the main hall, the bag on the floor to the right of the door as you exit the original house is in fact two bags occupying almost the same space. Depending upon which you click, they can give the false impression that things stored there have been removed.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
  - If an item you stored seems to have disappeared, move the crosshair around until you find the other bag.
- Sometimes a giant or attacking bandit spawns somewhere inside the walls of the house in the outdoor cell of Windstad Manor. They can be heard and it can be observed through the Detect Life effect and the Aura Whisper dragon shout, but not interacted with.
  - Leaving the cell (like entering the house) and returning usually moves the giant or the bandits outside the walls of the house.
- Sometimes the dead draugr from outside the nearby High Gate Ruins will spawn on the property.
- The barrel at the horse stables here may respawn when it wasn't supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The horkers near the hatchery were intended to become tame once the hatchery was built (or possibly only once it had started producing). Bugs in the related scripts make this very random, however, and they may become tame or hostile seemingly at random, or even some tame and some hostile.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.8, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=26495))
- Sometimes, all or some of the fish may disappear from the hatchery. Returning later will sometimes resolve this, albeit temporarily.
- You cannot mount fish on either of the two fish plaques added by the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") if you have already done so in another house. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing#Bugs "Skyrim:Fishing") for details.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Windward Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Dwelling.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Dwelling.png) | Nordic Dwelling: Windward Ruins ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windward+Ruins)) | | |

| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 5 |

Windward Ruins

**Windward Ruins** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever").

It is one of the three ruins visited for the quest [Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell"). With the [Vigil Enforcer Armor Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [Azarain](/wiki/Skyrim:Azarain "Skyrim:Azarain")'s corpse can be found here.

## Related Quests

- **[Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell")**: Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.
- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").
- **[Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set"): Investigate the mysterious disappearances of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

## Walkthrough

Windward Ruins interior

There is a central circular area surrounded by an enclosed outer passage. It is guarded by two [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") and contains an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") behind a tilted pillar by the outer wall of the passage. During the [Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials") quest, you will find a larger-than-life, ghostly skeever within the ruin. During the quest [Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell"), you will need to activate a plinth in the central area to place the book *[Power of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Power_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Power of the Elements")* received from [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"), then cast a [flame spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Fire Damage") at the plinth; you will then advance the quest and receive the clue to the second location. There is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush in the central area.

## Notes

- Three leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") have set up a camp 580 feet to the northwest below a rock ledge. The only items of note in the camp are an unlocked treasure chest and a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")*.
- [Agrane Peryval](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrane_Peryval "Skyrim:Agrane Peryval")'s camp can be found north of Windward Ruins if you have the [Saturalia Holiday Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Holiday_Pack "Skyrim:Saturalia Holiday Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed.

# Skyrim:Winterhold (region)

## Overview

This article is about the hold. For the city, see [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold").

.jpg)

The Winterhold region in the northeast corner of Skyrim

**Winterhold** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in northeast [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), with its capital in the city of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). It is initially affiliated with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), but can be captured by the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") after completing [Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav").

Winterhold is the northernmost hold in Skyrim, and has weather to match. The [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts") is off the northern coast, [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") is to the southeast, and [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is to the south and west.

Perhaps the most notable feature of Winterhold is the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), a fortress-like school for mages which was spared on a rocky outcropping even though the [Great Collapse](/wiki/Lore:Great_Collapse "Lore:Great Collapse") tore down most of the capital around it. All that remains of the once-great city are four still-standing buildings (and the collapsed remains of several others) near the entrance to the College.

Map of Winterhold

Winterhold, the hold capital

## Topographical Overview

Winterhold consists of snowy coasts and even snowier mountains. To the west and southwest is the Winterhold mountain range, which marks the border between Winterhold and [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), and some of the northern border with [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Between the mountains and the sea to the east lies a tundra, where the elements have rendered the landscape barren and lifeless. Rock and ice shelves, and occasionally shingle beaches, form the barrier between Winterhold and the sea to the north and east. To the north the tundra stretches out into the Sea of Ghosts, forming one of the most inhospitable environments in Skyrim.

### Flora and Fauna

Not many plants or creatures can survive Winterhold's harsh continental climate, and the hold is generally devoid of life as a result. The only plants that make their home in the mountains are the [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush and some [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). By the coast, [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") and [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") thrive. The area around the [Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War") is known to be rich in [fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish "Skyrim:Fish") and [dragonflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonfly "Skyrim:Dragonfly") and a large, isolated population of [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") can be found by the coast.

As for large fauna, only the hardiest of creatures make their home in Winterhold, such as [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear"), [snowy sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat"), and [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"). Occasionally, an unlucky traveler might also stumble upon an [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), or worse, a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother").

### Routes and Pathways

There is only one main road running through Winterhold. It originates as a branch of the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")-[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") road. It runs northward through the eastern side of the hold right to the city of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Another smaller and less used road runs from Winterhold to the ancient ruins of [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").

## Places

All locations in Winterhold with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for their significance.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold")** — A city on the northeast coast of Skyrim, and the capital of Winterhold hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold)
-  **[College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)")** — A school of the arcane arts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=College+of+Winterhold)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in Winterhold Hold, located southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and northwest of [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in Winterhold Hold, located northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and south of [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Stormcloak+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Bleakcoast Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakcoast_Cave "Skyrim:Bleakcoast Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakcoast+Cave)
-  **[Bloodchill Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") — A small cave southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing a subterranean vampiric player [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodchill+Cavern+%28CC%29)
-  **[Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") — A small island in the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Tooth+%28CC%29)
-  **[Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hob%27s+Fall+Cave)
-  **[Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") inhabited by [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Septimus+Signus%27s+Outpost)
-  **[Sightless Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Sightless_Pit "Skyrim:Sightless Pit")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sightless+Pit)
-  **[Stillborn Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stillborn_Cave "Skyrim:Stillborn Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stillborn+Cave)
- **[The Chill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chill "Skyrim:The Chill")** — The [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Jails "Skyrim:Jails") for [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), located on an island north-northeast of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and northeast of [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost"), across the sea. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Chill)
-  **[Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-northeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [Yngvild ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild_Ghost "Skyrim:Yngvild Ghost"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yngvild)

Mount Anthor, the highest peak in Winterhold
