### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

-  **[Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")** — A lighthouse west-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostflow+Lighthouse)
-  **[Great Lift at Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Alftand "Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand")** — A Dwarven lift to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") located northeast of [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") and southeast of [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Alftand)
-  **[Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly")** — A [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") northeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hela%27s+Folly)
-  **[Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench")** — A deep underwater ravine northwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") consisting of four submerged [shipwrecks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pilgrim%27s+Trench)
- **[Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts")** — A vast ocean to the north of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+of+Ghosts)
-  **[Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass")** — A [pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Passes "Skyrim:Passes") through the mountains in the southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wayward+Pass)
-  **[Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos")** — A [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") on a small island east of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+The+Pride+of+Tel+Vos)
-  **[Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War")** — A [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") east-southeast of [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum") and far northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Winter+War)

### Mines

-  **[Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine")** — A small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whistling+Mine)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic

-  **[Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alftand)
- **[Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach")** — An immense, naturally lit [cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by hordes of [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and containing the ruins of a [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackreach)
-  **[Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the tomb of [Warlord Gathrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironbind+Barrow)
-  **[Journeyman's Nook](/wiki/Skyrim:Journeyman%27s_Nook "Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook")** — A small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Journeyman%27s+Nook)
-  **[Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Saarthal)
-  **[Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand") — A Nordic ruin located north of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sivdur%27s+Respite+%28CC%29)
-  **[Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins")** — A small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") north of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") containing a [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skytemple+Ruins)
-  **[Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north-northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snow+Veil+Sanctum)
-  **[Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing the [shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Yngol's Shade") of an ancient Nord warrior. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yngol+Barrow)
-  **[Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Companion ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Companion_Ghost "Skyrim:Companion Ghost"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ysgramor%27s+Tomb)

-  **[The Serpent Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Serpent_Stone "Skyrim:The Serpent Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Serpent+Stone)
-  **[Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+of+Azura)
-  **[The Tower Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Tower_Stone "Skyrim:The Tower Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Tower+Stone)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Driftshade+Refuge)
-  **[Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") south of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Fellhammer)
-  **[Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") south of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") initially occupied by [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Kastav)
-  **[Snowpoint Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowpoint_Beacon "Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon")** — A small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snowpoint+Beacon)

### Unmarked Places

- There are four [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") in Winterhold.
  - A [Shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") near the [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp").
  - Three [Shrines of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines"):
    - East of [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave").
    - East of [the Tower Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Tower_Stone "Skyrim:The Tower Stone").
    - Northeast of [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb").

## Winterhold Quests

All quests that are started in or are related to Winterhold (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").

### Imperial Legion Civil War Quests

- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav")**: Take [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and rescue the prisoners within. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Kastav")**: Reclaim [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").
- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.

### College of Winterhold Quests

- All the [College of Winterhold quests](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") are related to Winterhold.

### Companions Quests

- **[Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")**: Retrieve the Fragments of Wuuthrad and wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

### Dark Brotherhood Quests

- **[Kill Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Deekus "Skyrim:Kill Deekus")**: Slay an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Deekus "Skyrim:Deekus") looting a shipwreck.

### Thieves Guild Quests

- **[Speaking With Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence")**: Track down the [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") behind the Guild's misfortunes.
- **[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")**: Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Toying With The Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Toying_With_The_Dead "Skyrim:Toying With The Dead")**: Retrieve a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil")'s journals for an interested buyer.

### Side Quests

- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Dawnguard Quests

- **[Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Bring the Elder Scrolls to [Dexion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus").
- **[Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Obtain information on the Dragon Elder Scroll.

### Creation Club Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.
- **[Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put a stop to two bandit gangs wielding strange otherworldly equipment.
- **[Creature of Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Creature_of_Legend "Skyrim:Creature of Legend")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Track down and tame the last living [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn").
- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.
- **[Guests for Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:Guests_for_Dinner "Skyrim:Guests for Dinner")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor"): Attend a feast.
- **[The Lost Library](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Library "Skyrim:The Lost Library")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories"): Locate a huge collection of powerful spell tomes.
- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").
- **[Swift as an Arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Swift_as_an_Arrow "Skyrim:Swift as an Arrow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack"): Learn how to craft and use [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow").

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests are located in Winterhold. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Winterhold "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

## Notes

- Winterhold is the only Hold that doesn't have a plot of land for sale if *Hearthfire* is installed, making [building a house](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") there impossible. As a result, it is also the only Hold where no [housecarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") are available. It doesn't matter if you helped [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") or not.

## Bugs

- Due to the fact that [Ramati](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati "Skyrim:Ramati"), [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani"), and [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi") at [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse") are part of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") crime faction, should you resurrect and re-kill them, then you could theoretically receive a bounty in that hold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is in the Winterhold crime faction, rather than the [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") one.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- Oddly, since the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") is marked as being owned by the Winterhold crime faction, if you help anyone in the hold (including [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and ironically enough, anyone from the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")), you will be able to take things from the longhouse without it being considered theft.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19319)) A new faction was created specifically for the residents of the longhouse in order to set ownership correctly.

## Overview

Winterhold Imperial Camp

**Winterhold Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Winterhold Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), located southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and northwest of [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").

The camp is normally commanded by [Legate Sevan Telendas](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Sevan_Telendas "Skyrim:Legate Sevan Telendas"), except during the related quest, at which point [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will assume command.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Sevan Telendas](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Sevan_Telendas "Skyrim:Legate Sevan Telendas") (commander)  [Imperial Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster")  [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier")  [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav")**: Take [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and rescue the prisoners within. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Winterhold Imperial Camp

It is a typical Imperial camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. To the south, in a row are the Legate's tent, command tent, and hospital tent. The Legate's tent contains an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. The command tent contains an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. The hospital tent contains six bed rolls, two of them occupied by wounded soldiers. Outside is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), a low table with a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and two random [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and an unlocked chest containing various items to treat the sick, including potions of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), potions of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease"), and [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Beside the tent are some barrels. West of the campfire are two rows of three small tents containing unowned bed rolls. Northwest of the fire is where the [Imperial quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster") works, in front of his tent. His workstation consists of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") , and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), with various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") on display on a table in front and inside his tent. North of the fire are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. There is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") near the fire, and a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush near the small tents.

Any time [Winterhold Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- Three ore veins are near the camp: a [moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") vein southwest of the camp, and two [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") veins northwest of the camp.

# Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp

## Overview

Winterhold Stormcloak Camp

**Winterhold Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Winterhold Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), located northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and south of [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum").

This camp will only be present if the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") hold [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") and the rest of Winterhold Hold, whether through martial might or via the negotiation during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") are camped here under the command of [Kai Wet-Pommel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kai_Wet-Pommel "Skyrim:Kai Wet-Pommel"), except during the related quest, when [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") takes command. Like similar military camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has no [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). Unlike most Stormcloak camps, it has no [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Kai Wet-Pommel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kai_Wet-Pommel "Skyrim:Kai Wet-Pommel") (commander)  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier")  [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

† This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Kastav")**: Reclaim [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Winterhold Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. Beside the campfire is an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"). Around the campfire are four small tents containing unowned hay piles. Next to one of the small tents is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), and next to another is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). West of the campfire, next to a stone pillar, is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the right of the hospital tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). Up the hill from the hospital tent is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. To the right of the commander's tent are some barrels. Up the hill from the commander's tent is the command tent, containing a lit brazier, a dresser, and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time.

Any time [Winterhold Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents.

## Notes

- A [Shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") can be found at this location if the camp isn't present.
- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") can be found southeast and northeast of this camp, respectively.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map displays the shrine; the previous one displayed the military camp.

Winterhold

**Winterhold** is a city on the northeast coast of Skyrim, and the capital of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") hold. It is initially aligned with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") under [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir"). It was once a large, bustling, and prosperous city. In [4E 122](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era#4E_122 "Lore:Fourth Era"), a cataclysmic event known as the "[Great Collapse](/wiki/Lore:Great_Collapse "Lore:Great Collapse")" occurred, in which most of the city fell into the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Lore:Sea_of_Ghosts "Lore:Sea of Ghosts"). Winterhold now only consists of a few rudimentary buildings and the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), one of the only original structures still standing. Many of the remaining local residents suspect the College caused the city's destruction, but the College insists the event was caused by the earthquake in [Vivec](/wiki/Lore:Vivec_(city) "Lore:Vivec (city)") and subsequent eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"). The few remaining residents of Winterhold can usually be found drinking their sorrows away in [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"); most of these characters can point you to local quests. Birna at [Birna's Oddments](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna%27s_Oddments "Skyrim:Birna's Oddments") can also sell you the [Coral Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Coral_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Coral Dragon Claw") for 50 septims, which you will need to further investigate [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

For more information on Winterhold, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Winterhold_(city) "Lore:Winterhold (city)").

## Notes

- With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, Winterhold is the only hold where you cannot buy or [build](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses"). As a result, it is also the only hold where you will not be offered the services of a [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), even as a bodyguard. Despite that, three [stone quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") will be present.
- Winterhold is set to experience a 100% chance of snowfall. It will always be snowing even if the [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") is used.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19800)) This has been altered to 99% snow storm and 1% cloudy, since the shout requires there to be a "pleasant" weather variety available. As a side effect of this, it will now be 1% possible in normal gameplay for Winterhold to have cloudy weather instead of a snow storm.
- There is no jail in Winterhold. Instead, criminals are exiled to a cave far to the north of the town called [The Chill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chill "Skyrim:The Chill"), guarded by four [frost atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"). [Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Guard "Skyrim:Winterhold Guard") will also mention this when you agree to go to prison by saying *"Ha. Enjoy the Chill."*
- Random soldiers of the opposing [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") faction may spawn near the town and attack the guards. Aiding the guards in killing the soldiers will count as an assault or murder, and the guards will turn hostile and attack.
- The guards patrolling the city don't carry the [Winterhold Guard's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Winterhold Guard's Shield"), as guards usually do, though there is one outside the city who does. The guard in question is the one who patrols the road near [Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. This particular guard NPC was set to inherit its inventory from a Stormcloak soldier variant different from guards elsewhere. This is also why the guards carried two-handed weapons, in addition to their lack of shields.
- Both [Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp") and [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp") are closer to other hold capitals than the city itself. Winterhold Imperial Camp is closer to [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and Winterhold Stormcloak Camp is closer to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
- Version 2.0.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces all [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes here with the snow-covered version of the same plant.
- Winterhold also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Winterhold "Arena:Winterhold") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.

## Bugs

- When paying a bounty in Winterhold, the guard will mention that stolen goods will be confiscated. However, no items will actually be lost, as there is no evidence chest anywhere throughout the hold.

:   - In [Skyrim Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"), stolen goods **are** removed when paying a bounty in Winterhold and are sent to the nearest Evidence Chest - in Dawnstar. However, stolen goods will not be removed when being sent to The Chill, as Winterhold itself still lacks an evidence chest.

# Skyrim:Witchmist Grove

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Grove.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Grove.png) | Grove: Witchmist Grove ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Witchmist+Grove)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 14 |
| Occupants | |
| [Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [Hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), [Moira](/wiki/Skyrim:Moira "Skyrim:Moira") the [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WitchmistGroveExterior | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |

Witchmist Grove

**Witchmist Grove** is a small shack north of [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") and south of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove").

The easiest way to reach the grove is to travel to Kynesgrove and head due south from there.

## Related Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

## Witchmist Grove

Witchmist shack interior

It is a small grove of trees with a doorless shack surrounded by sharpened stakes in the center. There are other typical hagraven markings around the area. A short distance to the north is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). Prior to starting the related [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember") a generic [witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") resides here. Once you initiate the quest it is changed to a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") named [Moira](/wiki/Skyrim:Moira "Skyrim:Moira"). Inside the shack is a single bed and two barrels; one contains [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and the other foodstuffs. The shack is in total disarray, with numerous human and animal bones, goat and skeever heads and antlers strewn across the floor. The whole shack is covered in blood splatters, although the bed is still usable. There is a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")* on the floor beside the bed, and a total of seven [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"). Outside and underneath the wooden stairs leading up to the entrance is an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. There are several [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flowers, [creep clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster") and patches of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") in the vicinity.

## Notes

- According to a [Development Map](/wiki/File:SR-map-Development_Map_02.png "File:SR-map-Development Map 02.png"), this location was at one point located in [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), northwest of [Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn").
- It seems to respawn automatically when initiating the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), even if that is less than the stated 10 day respawn time.
- Some of the hagraven feathers may clip through the floor, ending up on the ground underneath the shack.
- This is a good place to lure [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") from the nearby camps, as you can use the surrounding fence and small doorway to the house for defense, making it difficult for them to attack.

# Skyrim:With Friends Like These...

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Repay your debt to [the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and show you are willing to kill on command.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid"), on sleeping some time after completing [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") |
| Location(s): | [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack")   [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") |
| Reward: | [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), Word for the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout, Membership in the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") if you listen to her) =-1 (Astrid if you attack her) |
| ID: | DB02 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") | **Concurrent** The optional quest, [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial"), will become unavailable partway through the quest | **Next →** [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary")  *or*  [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") | | |

Three potential victims await your decision

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Receive a [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(DB) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (DB)") from a courier.
2. Go to sleep.
3. Kill a captive or the Dark Brotherhood's [leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid").
4. Choose to join or destroy the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").

### A Mysterious Note and a Good Night's Sleep

The Mysterious Note

Some time after [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") rewards you for killing [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") and you've left [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will approach you and deliver a [Mysterious Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(DB) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (DB)") bearing the ominous words *"We know."* The next time you sleep for any duration, you will *"awake after a full sleep"* to find that you have been mysteriously transported to unfamiliar surroundings. The quest can also sometimes be started after completing Aventus's quest by sleeping in any bed, even before receiving the Mysterious Note from the courier.

### Astrid's Test

You will awaken in an [abandoned shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") to a greeting from [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid"). She will calmly inform you that your killing of Grelod the Kind has pleased the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), but that, in doing so, you stole a contract belonging to the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother"), the Brotherhood's disembodied spiritual leader. Thus, you must repay your debt: *"A life for a life"*, as Astrid explains. She will tell you that you cannot leave the room until someone dies. The unpickable door to exit the shack is locked, and Astrid has the key.

You have the option of fulfilling the Night Mother's demand for a life by killing Astrid. Doing this will cause you to fail this quest and immediately start the [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") quest.

If you don't wish to kill Astrid, the room is also occupied by three bound captives. Astrid will inform you that *"One of these poor sods has a contract out on their life. Which one is it?"* It is up to you to figure out which and then carry out the job. You can refuse to carry out the job, but you can't avoid killing somebody.

When facing them, the captive to the left-hand side is [Fultheim the Fearless](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim_the_Fearless "Skyrim:Fultheim the Fearless"), a mercenary. He claims to be unaware of anyone in particular who would want him dead, but reasons that, being a sell-sword, any number of people could hold a grudge against him. When intimidated, he also admits, *"Maybe there were... times I got carried away? But war is war."*

The captive in the center is [Alea Quintus](/wiki/Skyrim:Alea_Quintus "Skyrim:Alea Quintus"), a crass and abrasive mother of six who constantly and irritatingly demands to be released. She indicates that the tough attitude she has adopted to manage so many children might motivate someone to wish her dead. *"Do some people look down on me? Have I made some enemies? You're damn right."*

The final captive, to the right-hand side, is a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") named [Vasha](/wiki/Skyrim:Vasha "Skyrim:Vasha"), who casually incriminates himself as an *"obtainer of goods, taker of lives, and defiler of daughters."* He is the only one of the three who remains calm in the face of imminent death, and mentions that this isn't the first time he's been *"bagged and dragged."* He also states that *"If one of my enemies wouldn't pay to have me killed, I'd take it as a personal insult."*

In truth, it doesn't matter which captive(s) you choose. You won't encounter any of them again (unless you return to the shack, and even then you won't be able to learn more). If you kill one or more of them, Astrid will give you the password to the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") "The Black Door". You will then be given a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack_Key "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack Key") to let yourself out of the shack. Alternatively, you can kill Astrid and loot the shack's key from her corpse.

| Victim(s) | Astrid's comments |
| --- | --- |
| Alea | *"Ah, the feisty goodwife. Quite the mouth on her. Someone must have wanted her dead... right?"* |
| Fultheim | '*"Oh ho. The whimpering Nord, eh? Yes, yes, I can see how you'd come to that conclusion. Interesting choice."* |
| Vasha | *"The conniving Khajiit. Cat like that was sure to have enemies. It's no wonder you chose him."* |
| Alea and Fultheim | *"The blubbering barbarian and the tenacious mother. Must have been one of them, right?"* |
| Alea and Vasha | *"Hmm. The fearless wife and mother, and the underhanded Khajiit. Had to be one of them, right? Interesting choice."* |
| Fultheim and Vasha | *"The timid warrior and the sly Khajiit. Must have been one or the other, right?"* |
| Alea, Fultheim, and Vasha | *"Well, well, aren't we the over-achiever? Three possibilities, three victims. Must have been one of them, right? So why take chances..."* |
| Astrid | *"Well done..."* |

### Enter the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary

The [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") is located almost due south of the Abandoned Shack, near the southern border of the province of Skyrim and just west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

:   Upon entering the Sanctuary, *the optional [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial") quest will fail if you started it, or be unavailable if you have not started it.* If you want to do this minor quest, detour to the quest location, north of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), on the way to the sanctuary.

When you activate the Sanctuary's entrance, The Black Door, it will ask, *"What is the music of life?"* Answer with the password Astrid taught you: *"Silence, my brother"*. You will be welcomed to your new "home" and the door will open.

### Speak Again with Astrid

Find Astrid inside. She will welcome you to the family by giving you several pieces of [Shrouded Armor apparel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), which provide enhancements useful to assassins. (There are also several other Shrouded Armor pieces on a shelf to the right of the room.) You are a now a full member of the Dark Brotherhood, and enjoy all the [advantages](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Advantages_to_Joining "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") associated therewith.

Astrid will reveal that she is currently arranging an important job to give you, and that you should, in the meantime, take care of some routine assassination contracts handled by [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"). She will encourage you to introduce yourself to your new family members and give a rundown on how the Brotherhood operates. She gives a brief history on the Brotherhood and also informs you that they have done away with all rules and policies except for one simple principle, "Respect the Family". You may also learn that the corpse of the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") is en route to the Sanctuary, though she does not know when it might arrive.

She finishes by again directing you to Nazir, assigning you your next quest, [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **With Friends Like These...** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- The key required to exit the Abandoned Shack will not appear in Astrid's inventory if you attempt to pick her pocket, but will only appear in her inventory if you kill her.
- The amount of time you choose to sleep just before Astrid takes you is irrelevant—no time will pass and your "Hours Slept" statistic will not be updated. After waking up in the Abandoned Shack, the [Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Rested "Skyrim:Rested") or [Well Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Rested "Skyrim:Well Rested") effect will still nevertheless be applied, unless you're a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy").
- After Astrid's initial speech and before killing any of the captives, you can attempt to pickpocket her if you have the [Misdirection](/wiki/Skyrim:Misdirection "Skyrim:Misdirection") perk. If you succeed, you can obtain a complete set of Shrouded Armor along with her [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe"). At the end of the Brotherhood quest chain, you'll get another Blade of Woe as the reward, making it possible to dual-wield them. If you choose to spare the captives and kill Astrid instead after pickpocketing her equipment, she will be an easy kill as she obviously won't be wearing her armor or weapon. On the other hand, if your pickpocket is high enough to steal these things, you're probably powerful enough in other ways to kill her even if she was wearing them.
- The rewarded Shrouded Armor consists of a set of [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Shrouded Boots"), a [Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl") and a pair of [Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"). This set is marked as [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor").
- If you start this quest before receiving the Mysterious Note, it will never be sent to you.
- An unused NPC with the name "[Player Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Player_Friend "Skyrim:Unused NPCs")" is associated with this quest, but was not implemented in the final release of the game. Pre-release reports for Skyrim claimed that the Dark Brotherhood would make you assassinate NPCs whom your character had befriended, which this NPC's association with this quest corroborates.
  - In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), earlier versions for some lines can be seen. Astrid's last line when you refuse to cooperate is normally *"Now it's time to face the consequences of your actions. You don't leave this shack until someone dies."*, but it's shown that the earlier version actually would've said *"Now it's time to face the consequences of your actions. So, kill a friend, then sleep, and I'll visit you once more. To finalize your repayment."* This line also corroberates the fact you would've had to kill an NPC you had befriended.
  - Similarly, [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") would normally say: *"There you are! Astrid's told me all about you. Heard she pulled the ole' "Choose your victim" gag with you. Ah, I love that one..."* when meeting you for the first time in the Sanctuary, but the earlier version goes as such: *"There you are! Astrid's told me all about you. I guess you did it, huh? You killed your friend? Trust me - you made the right decision."* This appears to be the only other line mentioning this earlier idea.
- All of the potential victims completely resist poison if you reverse-pickpocket some onto them, so they must be killed using either a weapon or spell.
- The map marker for the shack is only added after either Astrid gives you the key or you kill Astrid and loot it from her corpse, unless you have already found it prior to being brought there.
- No matter how you finish the quest, the Abandoned Shack will remain uninhabited, aside from the corpses of anyone you killed.
- Don't store anything in the Abandoned Shack, as the building resets every 10 days.
- If you choose to kill Astrid, any or all of the three captives can be untied and released after her death.
- Conversely, if you kill a captive first, Astrid becomes "essential" and unkillable, so it is impossible to kill her to get the Abandoned Shack key off her. She can be knocked down, and will revert to non-hostile (and full health) when she gets up again, so you can talk to Astrid to be given the key.
  - Also, once one of the captives is killed, you will never be given the option to release the remaining two - not even after leaving and re-entering the Abandoned Shack: they will remain there, bound and hooded, for all time unless you choose to murder them.
- If you kill one or two of the captives, you can talk to Astrid and hear one of the responses mentioned above. If you exit conversation without selecting any of the dialogue options and kill another one (or the third if you killed two before talking to her), Astrid will give a different response. Without reloading, you can hear up to three different responses this way.
- If you use the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") on any of the captives, it will still count as killing them, and the one you selected will be dead once the effect wears off.
- If you cast [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance_(spell) "Skyrim:Clairvoyance (spell)") inside the shack, it will always point to Vasha. This is due to the fact that the Clairvoyance spell will always target the last objective added in any given quest and should not be interpreted to mean that Vasha is the correct choice.
- If you cast [Reanimate Corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_Corpse "Skyrim:Reanimate Corpse") on a captive you killed, the captive will follow you inside the shack, but will disappear immediately once you exit.
- If you have *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* installed, sleeping inside [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon"), [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), or [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") will still cause you to wake up in the Abandoned Shack. Likewise, if you have *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* installed and sleep on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), or at your [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") with *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, you will get the same results. You can also encounter the same results if you install [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") content, depending upon what it is.
- The [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe") and a full set of Shrouded equipment ([Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), [Shrouded Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"), [Shrouded Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Shrouded Boots"), [Shrouded Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl")) can be obtained by killing Astrid if you choose not to join the Brotherhood.
- No matter how you finish the quest, [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") will still view you as his savior for getting rid of [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").
- Either joining the Dark Brotherhood or destroying it will prevent further [assassination attempts against you](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin_Sent_to_Kill_the_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions").
- Ironically, given the fact that they're already immobilized, all three captives are immune to [paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(effect) "Skyrim:Paralyze (effect)") effects. Astrid is immune to them as well.

## Bugs

- Any captives that are spared during the quest remain kneeling with their hood on indefinitely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If you choose to kill Astrid, the captives may simply disappear from the shack without a trace.
- If you read the Mysterious Note on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") and then read a Black Book afterwards, a bed may appear in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). **?**
- You may not receive the *Mysterious Note* after completing *Innocence Lost*. When encountering a courier, he will simply reply *"Nope, sorry. Nothing."*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - Sleep right after finishing the *Innocence Lost* quest (speaking with [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") for the second time). This may trigger the courier's delivery or your awakening inside the shack.
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and type `setstage DBEntranceQuest 20`. This should add the *Mysterious Note* to the courier, triggering its delivery and allowing you to continue the quest normally after sleeping.
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and type `setstage db02 10` to start the quest. Next, enter the command `player.moveto 1BDE8`. You will be transported inside the shack and the quest should proceed normally.
- Once you've killed all the captives, you may not be able to interact with Astrid. She will simply just say *"Brother"* and you can't start a conversation with her.
  - Reload a save from before she told you to kill one of the captives.
  - Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and type `stopquest DarkBrotherhood` and hit enter, then type `resetquest DarkBrotherhood` and hit enter.
- Sometimes the quest will not start after sleeping.
- Upon resting in bed you'll wake up inside the shack and start the dialogue normally, but when prompted to kill one of the captives, the game freezes, and any attempt to use the console or move is useless. Also, teleporting to the shack and manually starting the quest makes the game freeze when you exit the shack or enter any building.
- After getting the correct answer from Astrid, the Black Door will not provide it in the dialogue options when asking for it, thus preventing the player from entering the Sanctuary.
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and type `setpqv DarkBrotherhood BlackDoorPass_var 1`. This should add the correct dialogue option. Astrid may not be inside though, you can find her in the Abandoned Shack, and she will have correct dialogue options.
- If this quest is set to transport you to the Abandoned Shack while [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") is about to begin, that quest would be interrupted and potentially broken by the kidnapping scene.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| With Friends Like These... (DB02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Astrid, of the Dark Brotherhood, informed me that by killing Grelod the Kind, I have robbed her organization of a kill. I have been taken captive and moved to some remote shack. Astrid will only give me the key if I kill someone she has taken captive, to "repay my debt." *Objective 10:* Kill one of the captives |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Speak with Astrid |
| 40 |  | I have killed one of the captives as Astrid instructed, and must now gain entrance to the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary, which is located in the southern Pine Forest. Astrid has provided me with the correct passphrase - "Silence, my Brother." *Objective 40:* Enter the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Speak with Astrid |
| 200 | ☑ | I have killed an innocent person, gained entrance into the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary, and been officially welcomed into the Dark Brotherhood by Astrid. There's no turning back now. |
| 220 | ☒ | Astrid invited me into the Dark Brotherhood, but I killed her instead. I will now never be able to join the shadowy organization of assassins. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB02`.

# Skyrim:Wizard Duel

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Fend off and defeat a [challenger](/wiki/Skyrim:Challenger "Skyrim:Challenger").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Challenger |
| Location(s): | A city |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | WIChangeLocation03 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Skill rank of 50 in any school of magic | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Skill rank of 50 in any school of magic | | |

A challenger

## Quick Walkthrough

1. A [challenger](/wiki/Skyrim:Challenger "Skyrim:Challenger") appears.
2. Meet the challenger.
3. Accept or refuse the challenge.
4. Kill the challenger or flee.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Once you have a high level of skill in any [magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") school, upon entering a habitable location or exiting an inn after sleeping, a [challenger](/wiki/Skyrim:Challenger "Skyrim:Challenger") may appear and challenge you to a duel. Regardless of your answer, a combat ensues.

## Notes

- If you try to back out of the duel by saying "sorry", any nearby [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") will help you with your duel.
- If you do not use magic to fight the mage, he will taunt you by saying: "This is a mage's duel. You know magic!"
- If any of your [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") join in on the duel, he will order them to stop, explaining that it is supposed to be a one-on-one duel. This does not seem to affect the quest in any way, and companions will not abide to his demands. The same happens if other NPCs nearby are hit by his spells.
- This duel can lead to your expulsion from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). There is a [quest to rejoin](/wiki/Skyrim:Rejoining_the_College "Skyrim:Rejoining the College") if this happens.

## Bugs

- If you enter another cell while fighting against the Challenger, you will lose their location and be unable to finish this mini-quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you fight him with conjured weapons, the Challenger will still taunt you as if you weren't fighting him using magic.

## Quest Stages

| Wizard Duel (WIChangeLocation03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Kill Challenger |
| 101 |  | *Objective 100:* Kill Challenger |
| 200 |  | *(Challenger killed)* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIChangeLocation03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIChangeLocation03`.

# Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Wolfskull Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wolfskull+Cave)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Wolfskull_Cave "Lore:Wolfskull Cave")) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes (See [bugs](#Bugs)) |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 8 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") or [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Refugees "Skyrim:The Refugees")* [Necromancer's Ritual](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Ritual "Skyrim:Necromancer's Ritual")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") | |

| WolfskullCaveExterior, WolfskullCave01, WolfSkullCave02 | |

| West of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") Southeast of [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 1 |
| # of [Moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") | 1 |

Wolfskull Cave

**Wolfskull Cave** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") or [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains two zones: *[Wolfskull Cave](#Wolfskull_Cave)* and *[Wolfskull Ruins](#Wolfskull_Ruins)*.

The occupants of this cave vary depending upon whether the related quest, [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf"), is active. The cave is normally occupied by bandits, but the bandits are replaced by necromancers and their companions during the quest. The cave's standard boss chest is also unavailable during the quest. The second half of the dungeon, including the entire *Wolfskull Ruins* zone, is only accessible if the quest has been started.

## Related Quests

- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in Wolfskull Cave.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The path leads from the road to a rock face behind several bushes, including [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes. The cave entrance cannot be seen from the road. During the related quest, two [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") guard the entrance.

Above and just to the east of the entrance by two trees, there is a dead bandit, a large sack, and two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). To the right of the entrance, go up the slope and jump up the rocks to access the body, or climb down from the nearby [Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone").

One [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") is outside, 200 feet west-northwest of the entrance.

### Wolfskull Cave

The entrance leads into a natural tunnel lit by lanterns and torches. A few paces in, an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") lies on the ground. The first area has an empty cart, some bone chimes, and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the ground. There is a ledge high up on the right that will serve as your shortcut exit after completing the related quest.

Farther along, there is a second pickaxe, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and several empty wine bottles next to a patch of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungus. Shortly after, the path splits. The left-hand path descends and is patrolled by a bandit (or a draugr during the related quest). The ascending right-hand path leads over the left-hand path and onto a ledge above a chamber. By a campfire in the chamber below to the left, there is another bandit (or two necromancers during the related quest) that you can snipe. The chamber has a closed door.

Backtracking and taking the lower, left-hand path and following it into the same chamber, there are two more blisterwort and four [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungi along the passage and in the chamber. In front of the closed door, among both human and animal bones, is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a pickaxe. Around the campfire are many more empty wine bottles, a [rabbit haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_Haunch "Skyrim:Rabbit Haunch"), two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). An empty metal kettle sits in the fire.

Through the door is a flight of stairs leading down into another chamber containing two more bandits: one you can see to the right, while the other is farther to the right and out of sight. One of these is the boss. Off to the left is the boss chest.

During the related quest, the boss chest has been removed. Instead, the chamber past the door contains a leveled necromancer to the right, and a draugr magic-user and either an atronach or a skeleton to the left, on the far side of a sinkhole. A [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") grows from the lip of the hole. The only way to continue is to drop into the hole. If you drop from the northwest side of the hole, it is possible to land partway down on a ledge with two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). At the bottom of the sinkhole is some rubble, with a growth of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus near the start of a passage heading down to the northwest into the ruins.

### Wolfskull Ruins

There is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus at the start of this initial passage, and another on a wide ledge to the right overlooking a large cavern. A fort tower on the other side of the cavern has mystical energy weaving around it. The top of a shorter tower with a chest and potions is also visible from here. Many necromancers and draugr can be seen patrolling the fort and on the path beneath the ledge.

The passage continues downward, with more bleeding crown and fly amanita fungi, passing a pickaxe, then opening into a ruined chamber with two oil slicks on the ground and several oil lanterns hanging above. A necromancer patrols the area. This chamber contains another pickaxe, two blisterwort fungi, an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), and a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"). At the bottom of the chamber, the exit doorway has bone chimes and chains hanging down. A hanging moss is growing down the wall to the right.

Three flights of stairs lead down, where a difficult draugr and necromancer are patrolling. There are five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a woodcutter's axe on the landing of the first flight of stairs. At the bottom of the stairs is a doorway entering the base of a tower.

A spiraling stone staircase in the tower leads up to a circular room guarded by a draugr. An oil slick covers the floor, and an oil lantern hangs from the ceiling above. An iron battleaxe is on the ground by a candlelit stand. Beside this is some masonry with a satchel under it, and a random [poison of aversion to shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Potions") on it (although setting the oil on fire may cause the poison to scatter).

A doorway leads out of the tower onto a walkway, with stairs on the right leading down to another blisterwort fungus. Another draugr patrols the stairway leading upward.

Although difficult, it is possible to use the rocks on the left to jump onto the lip that runs around the battlements, and from there onto the tower you have just exited (seen from the initial ledge). An unlocked chest, a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), and a random poison of aversion to shock are on top of the tower.

Ahead is a large arch with a highly leveled draugr and a necromancer standing guard on top of the wall. Beneath the arch, stairs on the far side lead upward. Several more hanging moss in this area hang from the walls.

The path turns left and climbs more stairs. At the top is another leveled necromancer and a draugr. There are some patches of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") growing on the ground. The path turns to the south, where there is another woodcutter's axe on the ground among human bones. The path leads out onto a platform level with the original ledge where you entered. Two draugr patrol this area.

The path continues to another doorway at the bottom of another tower. Two necromancers stand partway up the next flight of spiral stone stairs, and three more are at the top, including one named [Ritual Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Ritual_Master "Skyrim:Ritual Master"). Once they are all dealt with, there is a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Refugees "Skyrim:The Refugees")* on the ritual pentagram at the top of this tower. With the [Necromantic Grimoire](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, a pedestal with a [Necromancer's Ritual](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Ritual "Skyrim:Necromancer's Ritual") spell tome can be found here.

To the southeast, a lever to the left of a raised wooden bridge will lower it. Across the bridge is an unlocked boss chest at the top of yet another tower, with stairs leading down to a passage into a room with a random scroll in the corner. A wooden door takes you back to *Wolfskull Cave* and the shortcut previously mentioned above the empty cart near the entrance.

## Notes

- Because the necromancers in the ritual area start as neutral, you can make the draugr kill the necromancers for you (see [bugs](#Bugs)). When you get to the final area and can just see the ruins and the swirling blue mists, shooting an arrow high over the heads of the necromancers will set them looking for enemies, then another arced high over the head of the draugr on the right of the tower will set him and the other draugr hunting. This will result in the two groups attacking each other, substantially reducing the opposition. Sometimes one or more of them will also converge on you, normally led by a high-level draugr who is initially standing on the wall over the large arch.
- Script notes attached to the related quest and its objectives indicate this location was at one point known as "**Wolfskull Caverns**" instead.

## Bugs

- If you are sent to Wolfskull Cave as part of a radiant quest (such as [Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights")), you will not be able to complete the radiant quest while The Man Who Cried Wolf is active. You will need to first finish The Man Who Cried Wolf, then wait for the dungeon to reset.
- Shooting arrows over the summoning circle and over the large arch to the right of the highest tower can cause several of the necromancers and draugr to attack each other.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- In order to clear this cave, you must enter it before The Man Who Cried Wolf is active and kill the bandit boss, who is in the ice cave section of the first zone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  -  The cave can be reverted to its clearable form after The Man Who Cried Wolf has been completed by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and entering the code `"000ABAB7".disable`.
  -  The cave can be manually set to "cleared" by entering the console command `SetLocationCleared 000192c8 1`.
- When the cave resets, the ritual to summon Potema may repeat itself. In addition, the swirling effect may return as well. **?**
- The navmesh on the exterior door into Wolfskull Cave is missing a door portal. This can cause NPCs to be unable to enter the dungeon at all.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Wolfskull Cave
- 

  Wolfskull Ruins
