# Skyrim:Word Wall

## Overview

The word wall at Ancient's Ascent

A **word wall** is a wall etched with a set of words in the [Dragon Language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language"). Multiple word walls can be found in various locations throughout Skyrim.

On each word wall one of these words may be highlighted. A highlighted word is a [word of power](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power"), that allows you to unlock one word in one of the [Dragon Shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Once you have found a word of power you must absorb a [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") soul to use the associated Dragon Shout.

## Locations

Most of the word walls are located in [Dragon Lairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") and [Nordic Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins"). There are two quests that help you discover new word walls:

- **[The Words of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power")**: Follow the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards")' advice to learn a [Word of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power") from a word wall.
- **[Shout - learn about word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout_-_learn_about_word_wall "Skyrim:Shout - learn about word wall")**: Explore a location and learn a [Word of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power").

You can only obtain one location at a time from each method, but you can use both methods at once. Neither source will ever direct you to a location that is potentially quest-locked (even if the quest is active), or to locations that are missing from their list ([Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") and [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze")).

## Word Wall Translations

The text shown on the word wall depends on how many words you've learned for that shout. For example, if you have already learned the first word in the shout [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") in [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud"), then if you visit either [Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit") or [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume"), the word wall will be for the second word. This means that the word wall's text changes, depending on which Word(s) you've already learned; the two exceptions are [Throw Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Throw_Voice "Skyrim:Throw Voice") ([Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint")) and [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") ([Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)")).

| Thu'um | Word Wall | Translation |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Transliteration |
| [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") | | |
| **Found in:** [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent"), [Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde"), and [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb") (atop the hill, quest locked) | | |
| **Raan** | QETHSEGOL V4RUKIV K9 SARVIRRA ZOK KRIN R1N ALUN W4 FON1R ODUS FROD 4RK OFAN OK SIL F4 OK DROG | (This) stone commemorates (the) horse Sarvirra, (the) most courageous animal ever to charge (the) snowy battlefields, and give his life for his lord. |

## Notes

- The choral part of the "Word Learned" sound effect is considered to be music and will not be heard if your music volume is set to zero.
- There are two ruined word walls that you are unable to learn from; one in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)") and one in the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn").[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")
- The "word wall" for Drain Vitality located in the Forgotten Vale is not a traditional ancient Nordic structure, but rather a large boulder with a single word carved into it.[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")

## Bugs

- Occasionally, when you approach a word wall from which you had previously learned a word, you will hear the chanting and sizzling sound that you normally hear from a word wall you've never visited.

# Skyrim:Worker's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Worker's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Worker%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MixwaterMillWorkersHouse | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill") | |

The front of the Worker's House

The **Worker's House** is an abandoned house at [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill").

It is located next door to [Gilfre's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre%27s_House "Skyrim:Gilfre's House") at [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill"), southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), southeast of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"), on the banks of [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River").

## Worker's House

Interior of house

This building was used to house the five workers at [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill"), until they all decided to join the civil war. The owner [Gilfre](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre "Skyrim:Gilfre") has plenty to say about them. The house itself is a single-roomed dwelling that has been stripped of most of its valuables and furnishing. Inside nothing is owned and everything is free to take. It has been left in a shocking state with an overturned chair and clutter all over the floor. Against the southwest wall, to the left of the entrance is a long wooden table and bench. There are four bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on the table, while above it, hanging from the ceiling are three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, three bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and three bunches of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). There is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel to the left and a basket containing [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") to the right. Further to the right are two more barrels, with two [potions of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top of one of them. Hanging from the ceiling above the barrels are two racks holding four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), with a second pheasant having fallen to the floor.

In the northern corner, the eastern corner and coming out of the northeast wall, to the left of the fireplace are three single unowned beds. They all have empty wooden [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of them. In front of the fireplace is a round wooden table and two chairs, with a bottle of Nord mead, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. There is a bottle of wine and three bottles of Nord mead on the mantelpiece, with another bottle of Nord mead on the hearth alongside a stand where a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") used to hang. On the floor by the hearth is an overturned kettle that contained four [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), that are now spread out from it and another food barrel to the right of the fireplace.

## Notes

- The house is never locked.
- A pheasant may be glitched into the floor by the table.

# Skyrim:World Interactions

## Overview

**World interactions** are random events that can occur as you explore [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). Some events force your involvement, others need you to make the first move or they will just pass by, and some do not require your involvement to complete. All unnamed [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") and [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") involved in encounters are leveled unless stated.

There are 149 *spawn points* where an event can occur; you will not experience an event at every location every time you go near it. Some events take place over a fairly large distance, as each part of the same event takes place. The event is determined a fair distance from the spawn point which, if correctly estimated, allows one to manipulate which event occurs. The first spawn point likely to be found is between [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") and [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery"), with its event border extending to just before the bridge out of Riverwood. Green dots on this wiki's [Skyrim Satellite Map](https://srmap.uesp.net/) can help you pinpoint where a random encounter is likely to take place.

While playing Skyrim, you may encounter many other combinations of animals and hostile NPCs fighting, however, there are only a few deliberately set to happen. Most hostile animals and NPCs have a large radius of detection that is perhaps a deliberate attempt at setting up more random encounters, saving game data by not having any additional scripts to handle.

Interactions added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), and [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") are annotated with "DG", "DB", and "CC" superscripts, respectively.

## Reactive Events

A few non-random events will occur as a result of your actions.

- **[An enemy's gratitude](/wiki/Skyrim:An_enemy%27s_gratitude "Skyrim:An enemy's gratitude")**: If you kill someone, a rival of that person may send you [one](/wiki/Skyrim:WIKill04ThanksLetter "Skyrim:WIKill04ThanksLetter") of [two](/wiki/Skyrim:WIKill04RewardLetter "Skyrim:WIKill04RewardLetter") letters of gratitude.
- **Apologize or combat**: Assaulted [*verification needed*] NPC or relative will demand an apology.
- **Invisible Child**: If you use [magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") near a [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") they will ask you to make them invisible.
- **[Revenge, Hired Thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Revenge,_Hired_Thugs "Skyrim:Revenge, Hired Thugs")**: If you kill someone, a member of their family may [hire thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Thug "Skyrim:Hired Thug") to kill you.
- **Shout - Guard says stop**: If you [Shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") near a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") they may approach and ask you to stop.
- **[Steal, Thugs hunt player](/wiki/Skyrim:Steal,_Thugs_hunt_player "Skyrim:Steal, Thugs hunt player")**: If you steal an item, an NPC from that location may hire thugs to teach you a lesson. You do not have to be seen by the victim for this to occur.

A few minor quests randomly start after specific actions have taken place.

- **[Buy Dwarven artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact")**: If you purchase a dwarven item in a shop a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Calcemo "Skyrim:Letter from Calcemo") may be sent via [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") asking you to bring it to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").
- **[Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance")**: A friend has died and left you a sum of gold. A [letter of inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Inheritance "Skyrim:Letter of Inheritance") will be sent via courier to inform you of the tragic event.
- **[Scare my Enemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Scare_my_Enemy "Skyrim:Scare my Enemy")**: If you assault someone bare-handed, a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Request_from "Skyrim:Request from") may be sent from an NPC asking for a favor.
- **[Shout - learn about word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout_-_learn_about_word_wall "Skyrim:Shout - learn about word wall")**: If you Shout, then a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_a_Friend "Skyrim:Letter from a Friend") may be sent via courier to tell you about an important place.

## Reactions

The following random events occur in settlements as a direct result of an action that has been performed.

| Encounter Name | Details | Options | Requirements |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Accidentally dropped this** | An NPC may rush up and return your item. | None, the item is placed in your inventory. Responses by [voicetype](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-VoiceTypes "Category:Skyrim-VoiceTypes"): FemaleChild, FemaleCommoner, FemaleOldKindly, FemaleYoungEager, MaleBrute, MaleChild, MaleCommoner and MaleCommonerAccented, MaleOldKindly, MaleYoungEager | Drop an item of value. |
| **"Can I have that armor?"** | An NPC may approach and ask you if they can have the item. | If you reply yes they will pick it up, and their disposition to you will rise to 1 if it was 0. If you say no they will leave it alone; it is not necessary for you to pick it back up. Responses by voicetype: FemaleCommoner, FemaleCoward, FemaleYoungEager, MaleBrute, MaleCommoner and MaleCommonerAccented, MaleCoward, MaleDrunk, MaleYoungEager  Responses by voicetype if you tell them it's theirs: FemaleCommoner, FemaleCoward, FemaleYoungEager, MaleBrute, MaleCommoner and MaleCommonerAccented, MaleCoward, MaleDrunk, MaleYoungEager  Responses by voicetype if you tell them to leave it alone: FemaleCommoner, FemaleCoward, FemaleYoungEager, MaleBrute, MaleCommoner and MaleCommoner Accented, MaleCoward, MaleDrunk, MaleYoungEager | Drop a piece of armor or clothing. |
| **Child scares NPCs** | A [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") tries to surprise an adult. | None. | Tell a child they are invisible (after using magic near them). |
| **"Did you find something good?"** | An NPC may approach and comment on something you have just picked up. | Listen. Responses by voicetype: FemaleChild, FemaleCommoner, FemaleYoungEager, MaleChild, MaleCommoner and MaleCommonerAccented, MaleDrunk, MaleYoungEager | Pick something up. |
| **Drop weapon, Guard extorts**[†](#intnote_1) | A [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") may approach and tell you it is dangerous to leave weapons lying about. | If you say you "don't care" they will threaten you with jail and demand a 50 gold bribe. Refusing the bribe results in a bounty of 10 gold. To avoid such actions you should apologize and pick the weapon back up. | Drop a weapon. |
| **Fight over item** | Up to five NPCs will have an argument over a dropped item until a guard intervenes. (They may kill each other.) | Watch. | Drop an item, but not in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). |
| **Gift from a Friend**[†](#intnote_2) | An NPC with a friendly [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") may give you a gift. | Keep, drop, or sell the gift the NPC gave you. Responses by voicetype before they give you your gift: FemaleArgonian, FemaleChild, FemaleCommander, FemaleCommoner, FemaleCondescending, FemaleCoward, FemaleDarkElf, FemaleElfHaughty, FemaleEvenToned, FemaleKhajiit, FemaleNord, FemaleOldGrumpy, FemaleOldKindly, FemaleOrc, FemaleShrill, FemaleSultry, FemaleYoungEager, MaleArgonian, MaleBrute, MaleChild, MaleCommander and MaleNordCommander, MaleCommoner and MaleCommonerAccented, MaleCondescending, MaleCoward, MaleDarkElf, MaleDrunk, MaleElfHaughty, MaleEvenToned and MaleEvenTonedAccented, MaleKhajiit, MaleNord, MaleOldGrumpy, MaleOldKindly, MaleOrc, MaleSlyCynical, MaleSoldier, MaleYoungEager | Level 5 |
| **Just throw trash** | If you drop a very low value item, you may either overhear an NPC, or they may approach you and criticize you for littering. | Listen (and optionally) pick the item back up. Responses by voicetype when seen littering: FemaleArgonian, FemaleCondescending, FemaleDarkElf, FemaleElfHaughty, FemaleKhajiit, FemaleOldGrumpy, FemaleShrill, MaleArgonian, MaleCondescending, MaleDarkElf, MaleElfHaughty, MaleKhajiit, MaleOldGrumpy, MaleOrc, MaleSlyCynical | Drop an item. |
| **Rummaging through trash** | An NPC may comment on you looking inside or taking something from a 'rubbish container'. | Listen (and optionally) loot the container. Responses by voicetype when seen looking through trash: FemaleCondescending, FemaleElfHaughty, FemaleNord, FemaleOldGrumpy, MaleCondescending, MaleElfHaughty, MaleNord, MaleOldGrumpy  Responses by voicetype when seen taking something: FemaleCommoner, FemaleEvenToned, FemaleOldKindly, FemaleYoungEager, MaleCommoner and MaleCommonerAccented, MaleEvenToned and MaleEvenTonedAccented, MaleOldKindly, MaleYoungEager | Take something from or look inside a knapsack, barrel, sack, small sack or large sack. |

[†](#note_1)When the guard extorts you for 50 gold, the dialogue will work even if you don't actually have 50 gold on you. The script, however, will still deduct 50 gold which can lead to integer underflow issues on your gold amount.

- The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_2)The dialogue from this random encounter is intended to be spoken by the NPC designated as your friend, but is available to every NPC in the loaded area.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

### Beneficial Encounters

These are encounters where the only outcome is beneficial to you, or at the very least, do not have any sort of hostile outcome under any circumstance. The rewards can take any form, be that an enchanted weapon, a new location to discover, or simply knowing you have helped someone. If you choose to attack any of the participants, they will turn hostile.

| Encounter Name | Details | Options | Requirements |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Adventurer on the Way to Nearby Dungeon** | A [mercenary](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary_(wilderness) "Skyrim:Mercenary (wilderness)") is on the way to investigate a location. | You can [persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") them to tell you the location. The location given is just marked but not part of any quest. | Level 5 |
| **Arguing about Haknir**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | A [pirate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate") and [pirate mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Mage "Skyrim:Pirate Mage") arguing over treasure. |  | On Solstheim. |
| **Babette on the Road Near a Body**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") feeding on an adventurer. |  | Between 10pm and 5am, [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") complete |
| **Bandit Killed With Horse Left Behind** | An idle [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"), with a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") usually by its feet or hidden in the undergrowth. | The horse is free to ride. It travels when you fast travel, but won't stay in one place. | None |
| **Bard at rest** | [Talsgar the Wanderer](/wiki/Skyrim:Talsgar_the_Wanderer "Skyrim:Talsgar the Wanderer") resting by the side of the road. | You can pay him to [sing a song](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances"). | Talsgar is alive. |
| **Bard travelling on the road** | [Talsgar the Wanderer](/wiki/Skyrim:Talsgar_the_Wanderer "Skyrim:Talsgar the Wanderer") traveling the roads of Skyrim. | You can pay him to [sing a song](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances"). | Talsgar is alive. |
| **Bitten by a vampire**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | A [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") approaches and asks for a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") to cure himself after being bitten by a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). | If you have a [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease") you can heal him; you'll gain 100 gold and be able to trade with him once again. If not, he will run off in a panic. Only a found or purchased potion will work; one created using [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") won't. A map marker for a vampire lair will be added as well. | None |
| **College Application Denied** | An [Aspiring Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Aspiring_Mage "Skyrim:Aspiring Mage") attempts to reanimate a small [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). | Talking to him will give options to acquire a [Leveled Reanimation Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves#Reanimate "Skyrim:Staves"). | Level 15 |
| **Corpses in the aftermath of a dragon attack, Dog left behind** | Three burnt corpses around a [carriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage"). A [stray dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Stray_Dog "Skyrim:Stray Dog") nearby and possibly a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). | Lootable chest in the carriage. | [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") complete |
| **Courier Delivering an Important Message** | A [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") taking a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Courier's Letter") to an investor. | Reading the letter adds a map marker. To read the letter you can persuade the courier to give it to you, kill him, or read it while pickpocketing him (it is not necessary to take it). | None |
| **Courier Has Mail For You** | A [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") stops you in your tracks, delivers you a letter (or a series of letters), and leaves. | Read the letter (or letters) the courier gave you. | Varies by letter |
| **Courier on the Run** | An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Courier "Skyrim:Imperial Courier") or [Stormcloak courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Courier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Courier") running along the road. |  | [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front "Skyrim:A False Front") not active |
| **Cragslane** | Three [pit wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Pit_Wolf "Skyrim:Pit Wolf") near a dead NPC. | The NPC carries a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Note "Skyrim:Small Note") which adds [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") to your map. | None |
| **Dark Elf on Pilgrimage to Azura's Shrine** | [Faldrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldrus "Skyrim:Faldrus") walking to the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura"). | Talking to him will reveal the shrine's location. | None |
| **Dead Treasure Hunter with instructions** | A dead [treasure hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Hunter_(dead) "Skyrim:Treasure Hunter (dead)") with a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Hunter%27s_Note "Skyrim:Treasure Hunter's Note") that mentions a dungeon with a leveled enchanted weapon. | The note adds a marker for a dungeon (other than a Dragon Lair) | None |
| **Drinking Companions** | Three [revelers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reveler "Skyrim:Reveler") offer you some [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"). | Offering [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") results in insulting the brand. Offering [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") results in a [Charmed Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Necklace "Skyrim:Charmed Necklace"). Having neither results in a Honningbrew Mead. | None |
| **Dwemer Junk Peddlers** | Two children, [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(child) "Skyrim:Sond (child)") and [Bottar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bottar "Skyrim:Bottar"), approach and try to sell some Dwemer junk. | Asking about where they got the junk will add [Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing") for 1 gold. | None |
| **Farmer leading Painted Cow to Giant Camp** | A [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(NPC) "Skyrim:Farmer (NPC)") (00106a61) leads a [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") to a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps"). | If you talk to him, he will tell you to stay away. After further questioning he will explain that he is taking the cow to a giant's camp, and that they might mistake you for a part of the offering. He advises you to keep your distance. You can then either wish him good luck, offer your help, or probe for further information. Probing further, he will explain that an annual offering keeps the giants away from his livestock, and that the paint signifies that the cow is being given willingly, adding that some people consider it to be a superstition. If you talk to him afterwards he will state that he is going to the inn, and the same three options as before appear.  If the cow is killed he will only state that his wife is going to kill him when she finds out. Killing the cow does not make the farmer hostile, and, if attacked, he will draw a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") but run away. If you follow him he will eventually end up in a giant's camp. If he gets too near to a giant they will attack him, however they will not attack the cow. | [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") or [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") |
| **Farmer refugees after dragon attack** | A [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(NPC) "Skyrim:Farmer (NPC)") (001034e4) and his wife (001034e6) either walking along the road, or resting in an inn, after their farm was destroyed by a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). | You can choose to give the farmers 5 gold, or say you have no gold to spare. | Level 4 |
| **Finding the Gourmet**[†](#intnote_3) [†](#intnote_4) | [Balbus](/wiki/Skyrim:Balbus "Skyrim:Balbus"), an aspiring cook, is wandering Skyrim looking for the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet"). | You can tell him you're the Gourmet, but you will need the [Gourmet's writ of passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage") to prove it. If you prove yourself to be the Gourmet, he will give you a fork and some rare ingredients. | Balbus still alive and [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") finished. |
| **Frostmoon Invitation**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | A Hunter directs you to [Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag"). |  | You are a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"). |
| **Giant leading a painted cow to camp** | A [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") leads a [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") towards a [giant's camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps"). |  | [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") or [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") |
| **Gift of flight**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")[†](#intnote_5) | A [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wizard "Skyrim:Wizard") experiments with flight. | No interaction possible. | On Solstheim. |
| **Headless Horseman** | The [Headless Horseman](/wiki/Skyrim:Headless_Horseman "Skyrim:Headless Horseman") appears and travels across Skyrim towards [Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest"). | No interaction possible. | Between 10pm and 5:30am |
| **Hey you there, take this**[†](#intnote_6) | A [fugitive](/wiki/Skyrim:Fugitive "Skyrim:Fugitive") approaches and foists an enchanted item upon you and runs off. Then a [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") approaches and asks about the fugitive. | Return the item for a single coin and betray the fugitive, keep the item and betray the fugitive, or keep the item and fool the hunter. The fugitive does not take the item back if still alive. Talking to the hunter after your first dialogue just yields generic hunter dialogue and no further interaction. | Level 2 |
| **Hook, Afflicted Refugee Headed to High Rock** | [Afflicted Refugee](/wiki/Skyrim:Afflicted_Refugee "Skyrim:Afflicted Refugee") fleeing Skyrim. | Adds a marker for the [Shrine of Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite") when talked to. | Level 10 and before stage 10 of [The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure") |
| **Hunter and Dog in the Wilderness**[†](#intnote_7) | A [Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") and a [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"). | Talking to hunters yields generic hunter dialogue, such as*"I've been hunting and fishing in these parts for years."* Can be asked what they have for sale. | None |
| **Hunters chasing**[†](#intnote_7) | Two [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") hunting a [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer"). | Talking to hunters yields generic hunter dialogue, such as*"I've been hunting and fishing in these parts for years."* No other interactions available. | None |
| **Looking to join Imperials** | A [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") (000bd759) (named Bodryn) walking to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") | When attempting to talk to him for the first time, he explains that he is on his way to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to join the Imperial Legion, because he believes that *"A united Empire is better for everyone."* Attempting to talk to him further yields one of two responses, either *"I was born and raised in Skyrim, but the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") treat us like dirt,"* or *"I want to be on the right side."*  Attacking him results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. If you follow him, he will eventually reach Solitude and disappear while going through the front gate. | Civil War not finished |
| **Looking to join Stormcloaks** | An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") (named Sylvian) walking to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") to join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") | When attempting to talk to him for the first time, he explains that he is on his way to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") to join the Stormcloaks, because he believes that*"Ulfric has the right of it."* Attempting to talk to him further yields one of two responses, either *"I may be Imperial, but Skyrim's just as much my home as any Nords',"* or *"The Empire is in shambles. They've banned the worship of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos")."*   Attacking him results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. If you follow him, he will eventually reach Windhelm and disappear while going through the front gate. | Civil War not finished |
| **Magic Student** | A [student](/wiki/Skyrim:Student "Skyrim:Student") appears and [requests help](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Student "Skyrim:Magic Student") in learning how to use [ward spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward#Spells "Skyrim:Ward"). | The student wishes to learn how to use ward spells by seeing one being used properly, by you. Once you have completed his request he departs, in the hope of finally gaining acceptance into the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). | Any settlement except [Orc Strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") |
| **M'aiq the Liar** | [M'aiq the Liar](/wiki/Skyrim:M%27aiq_the_Liar "Skyrim:M'aiq the Liar") appears, and proceeds to dispense his words of wisdom. | Listen to his words and try to understand their meaning. Fishy sticks, werebears, and thinking outside the box and/or the other side of the 4th wall may be required. | None |
| **Mistwatch Escapee** | A [Frightened Woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Frightened_Woman "Skyrim:Frightened Woman") approaches and says she has escaped from [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") and asks for help. | Direct her to the nearest city. Mistwatch will be added to your map if you have not already found it. | None |
| **Netch Hunting Party**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | Join a group of hunters who are hunting [Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch"). | You can join them on the hunt or wish them luck and leave. | On Solstheim. |
| **Nobles *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Traveling with Bodyguard** | A [Noble](/wiki/Skyrim:Noble "Skyrim:Noble") riding a horse and escorted by a bodyguard. | If talked to, the Noble will be rude and warn you to leave, threatening to call his guard on you if you do not. This is a bluff, however, as he never does unless directly attacked. | None |
| **On the way to the Wedding** | [Plautis Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Plautis_Carvain "Skyrim:Plautis Carvain") and his wife [Salonia Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Carvain "Skyrim:Salonia Carvain"), with their [bodyguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodyguard_(Carvains) "Skyrim:Bodyguard (Carvains)") travel to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to attend a [wedding](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death"). | The player can act as a highwayman and demand they hand over their wedding presents, starting a fight. Looting them grants you expensive jewelry and gems. | Bound Until Death not started |
| **Vigilants Patrol**[†](#intnote_8) | Two [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr") patrolling the roads of Skyrim. | Due to bugs, they might turn hostile if healed or beneficial illusion magic is cast upon them. Adds [Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant") to your map if you ask them who they are. | None |

[†](#note_3)After your first encounter with him, Balbus may stay where he is for the rest of the game. As this position will normally be a typical location for random encounters, he may be killed if you trigger another encounter at that spot.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. Balbus will now unload properly after you leave the area.

[†](#note_4)The random encounter with Balbus may still not shut down due to the alias not registering itself to stop the scene when Balbus unloads.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. In addition to fixing this, the scene will no longer run if he has given you the Gourmet reward, or if he has been killed at some point.

[†](#note_5)This random encounter is a reference to [Tarhiel](/wiki/Morrowind:Tarhiel "Morrowind:Tarhiel") and his [Scrolls of Icarian Flight](/wiki/Morrowind:Scroll_of_Icarian_Flight "Morrowind:Scroll of Icarian Flight") in *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind")*. It will only happen once.

[†](#note_6)The item the Fugitive gives you in this random encounter is never tagged as stolen, allowing you to sell it if you wish.

[†](#note_7)The hunters in these random encounters may attack your [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"), even though your horse is your ally.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. This was due to incomplete faction relationships.

[†](#note_8)The Vigilants will attack [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") on sight if they see him following you during [A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend"). Unfortunately, since Barbas is invulnerable, they will perish.

### Encounters With Differing Outcomes

Hostilities may break out in the following encounters, but can be avoided depending on your actions and faction relations.

| Encounter Name | Details | Options | Requirements |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **A Good Death**[†](#intnote_9) | An [old Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Orc "Skyrim:Old Orc") stands idle near two dead [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat"). | When talking to him he asks if you are able to give him a good death. You can choose to fight him. | Level 5 |
| **Bandits dressed as Imperial Soldiers** | Three [bandits dressed as Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Soldier "Skyrim:Soldier") will attempt to extort money from you, three Imperial soldiers lie dead nearby. | You can pay the money, persuade them to let you go, expose or taunt them if you're in either the Legion or Stormcloaks respectively, or kill them. | None |
| **Bounty Collector\_Bounty Collector** | A [bounty collector](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_Collector "Skyrim:Bounty Collector") comes to retrieve the bounty on your head sometime after you have acquired a bounty in a hold (last visited a hold where bounty is). | Pay up or kill the collector. | 1000 gold bounty in a hold |
| **Dawnguard Outrider**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | You encounter [Saliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Saliah "Skyrim:Saliah") on the road. | She will only tell you to *"Stand Aside!"* if you get in her way. She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Cache_Key "Skyrim:Dawnguard Cache Key") and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Orders_-_Saliah "Skyrim:Dawnguard Orders - Saliah") that gives access to Dawnguard supply caches. Will be hostile if you are a vampire. | Complete either [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") for the [Volkihar vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan") or [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). |
| **Dawnguard Vampire Hunting**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | Three members of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") out at night searching for vampires. | Will be hostile if you are a vampire. Otherwise they will yield only generic Dawnguard dialogue. | Between midnight and 5am after choosing a side in the Dawnguard add-on |
| **Dragon fly by** | A non-aggressive [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") flies overhead. | A dragon flies by overhead, often attacking the wildlife, but never turning hostile. It is possible to hit it and make it aggressive, resulting in it attacking you, however it will never land.  The only way to make it land is to use the [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shouts "Skyrim:Shouts"). It will land, but only for the shortest amount of time possible. You will need to continuously use the shout to keep the dragon grounded while you fight it. | Completed Dragon Rising |
| **Imperial Scout Patrol** | Three [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") scouts traveling. | Trying to talk to them results in generic Imperial soldier dialogue, such as *"Can't wait to kill another of [Ulfric's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") boys"*  If you hang around them for too long, or you are a Stormcloak, they will get suspicious and warn you to back off. If you ignore the warnings to go away, they will eventually attack you. Attacking them results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. They will not grow suspicious if you are part of the Legion, however. | None |
| **Imperials on the Road** | Three [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") (00016942) on patrol. | Trying to talk to them results in generic Imperial soldier dialogue, such as *"Can't wait to kill another of [Ulfric's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") boys"*  If you hang around them for too long, or you are a Stormcloak, they will get suspicious and warn you to back off. If you ignore the warnings to go away, they will eventually attack you. Attacking them results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. They will not grow suspicious if you are part of the Legion, however. | None |
| **Imperials vs Stormcloaks** | Three [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") fighting three [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). | You may join in the battle or simply observe. Be advised however that attacking either side may result in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in, depending on the occupation status of the current hold and which side you attack. Trying to talk to them after the battle results in generic Imperial/Stormcloak soldier dialogue, such as *"Can't wait to kill another of [Ulfric's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") boys"* or *"I long to be out there, waging war against the Empire"* respectively.  If you hang around the victors for too long, or you are a member of the opposing faction, they will get suspicious and warn you to back off. If you ignore the warnings to go away, they will eventually attack you. They will not grow suspicious if you are part of the winner's faction, however. | None |
| **Imperials with Stormcloak Prisoner**[†](#intnote_10) [†](#intnote_11) | Three [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") soldiers escorting a Stormcloak prisoner. | If you get too close to the Imperials they will become suspicious and warn you to leave. They will turn hostile after repeated warnings, or if you set the prisoner free. You may either heed their warnings and leave them be, or help the prisoner escape. If you choose to help the prisoner, you can either set him free, or give him items and set him free *(Note: do not give him armor, as he will not equip it.)*. He will only defend himself if attacked and is quite weak and low on health. | None |
| **Scavenger** | A [scavenger](/wiki/Skyrim:Scavenger "Skyrim:Scavenger") looting the bodies of two Imperial soldiers and three Stormcloak soldiers, with one of the Imperials already looted. | Getting too close turns him hostile | None |
| **Skooma Dealer** | A [Skooma Dealer](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma_Dealer_(NPC) "Skyrim:Skooma Dealer (NPC)") (named for their race) attempts to sell you [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). | Accepting will allow you to buy some skooma from the Skooma Dealer. Questioning the legality of the product will result in combat. You can also attempt to intimidate the dealer into handing over their skooma; failure also results in combat. | None |
| **Stormcloak Scout Patrol** | Three Stormcloak scouts traveling. | Trying to talk to them results in generic Stormcloak dialogue, such as *"I long to be out there with my brothers, waging war against the empire"*  If you hang around them for too long, or you are a member of the Imperial Legion, they will get suspicious and warn you to back off. If you ignore the warnings to go away, they will eventually attack you. Attacking them results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. They will not grow suspicious if you are a Stormcloak, however. | None |
| **Stormcloaks on the Road** | Three Stormcloak soldiers on patrol. | Trying to talk to them results in generic Stormcloak dialogue, such as *"I long to be out there with my brothers, waging war against the empire"*  If you hang around them for too long, or you are a member of the Imperial Legion, they will get suspicious and warn you to back off. If you ignore the warnings to go away, they will eventually attack you. Attacking them results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. They will not grow suspicious if you are a Stormcloak, however. | None |
| **Taunting Adventurer** | An [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Taunting_Adventurer "Skyrim:Taunting Adventurer") insults you. | Taunting the adventurer back turns him or her hostile. | None |
| **Thalmor traveling on the road** | Three [Thalmor Justiciars](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Justiciar "Skyrim:Thalmor Justiciar") traveling. | Upon speaking to any of them they will become confrontational (but not hostile) unless there's *"Something you'd like to confess, perhaps?"* Confessing yourself as a Talos worshipper, saying that people should worship whatever they want, or remaining silent will turn them hostile. Attacking them preemptively results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in. | None |
| **Thalmor vs Stormcloaks** | Three Thalmor Justiciars fighting three Stormcloak soldiers. | If the Stormcloaks win (rare) trying to talk to them results in generic Stormcloak dialogue, such as *"I long to be out there with my brothers, waging war against the empire."*  If the Thalmor win as is usually the case, trying to talk to them results in generic, condescending Thalmor dialogue. Either way, If you hang around them for too long, they will get suspicious and warn you to back off. If you ignore the warnings to go away, they will eventually attack you (unless you're a Stormcloak and the Stormcloaks win). Attacking either side results in a bounty in whichever [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") you are in, though is cleared once the last witness from that side dies. | None |
| **Thalmor with Prisoner** | Three [Thalmor Justiciars](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Justiciar "Skyrim:Thalmor Justiciar") escorting a [prisoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Prisoner "Skyrim:Thalmor Prisoner"). | If you get too close to the Thalmor they will become suspicious and warn you to leave. They will turn hostile after repeated warnings, or if you set the prisoner free. Unlike the aforementioned *Imperials with Prisoner* encounter however, conversation with the Thalmor is possible, though as is typical of the Thalmor they are confrontational and rude. You may inquire about the prisoner, though they will rudely tell you to mind your own business, unless there's *"Something you'd like to confess, perhaps?"* Confessing yourself as a Talos worshipper, saying that people should worship whatever they want, or remaining silent will turn them hostile. If you choose to help the prisoner, you can either set him free, or give him items (as before, it is inadvisable to give him armor since he will not equip it) and set him free. He will only defend himself if attacked and is quite weak and low on health. | None |
| **Thieve's *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Guild Holdup** | A [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(wilderness) "Skyrim:Thief (wilderness)") approaches and demands your valuables | Offers some gold/goods if wearing Thieves clothes. Offers you your cut if wearing Nightingale clothes. The thief can be made to offer either if you belong to either faction, but are not wearing the corresponding attire.  Otherwise, you may either pay some gold, try to intimidate them, or turn them hostile by saying you don't have time for this. (Exiting the conversation has the same response.) You may also choose the persuasion check "Do I look like I have any coin?", which if you pass the thief will not become hostile. If you fail, the thief will tell you "I'm not going to ask again" and you'll get one more chance to respond. You may also sheath your weapon when attacked to turn the thief non-hostile no matter what dialogue choice you made. | None |

[†](#note_9)This random encounter does not properly unload and remove the Old Orc and the two sabre cats if you kill him, or if you ignore him and leave the area.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_10)This random encounter is never properly disabled if the Stormcloaks win the War, as the Imperial soldiers won't have someone to report to anymore.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_11)The Stormcloak Prisoner being escorted by Imperials may engage you in combat if the soldiers are attacked.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. The prisoner now has a combat override package list assigned that should prevent them from engaging at all.

### Hostile Encounters

The following are encounters where you have no option but to fight. The non-hostile party in some of these quests may win the fight, even without your aid. All NPCs or creatures encountered in hostile encounters are leveled unless otherwise noted.

| Encounter Name | Details | Requirements |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **4-Man Bandit Band**[*verification needed — need actual encounter name*] | A group of four [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), which can include males and females, will begin walking to their destination. It is possible to avoid combat by not approaching the bandits, but they will all turn hostile to you if you approach too closely or the bandit band enters into combat with anything else they encounter. | None |
| **Aggressive Adventurer** | An [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggressive_Adventurer "Skyrim:Aggressive Adventurer"), named for their race, attacks. | Level 5. |
| **Animals attacking bandit** | Two animals ([skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), or sabre cats) attacking a single bandit. | None |
| **Animals attacking reaver**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | Two animals (wolves, [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), [snowy sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat"), [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear"), or [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll")) attacking a single [reaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver#One-Handed_Melee_Fighters "Skyrim:Reaver"). | On Solstheim. |

[†](#note_12)This random encounter may occur after you collect all of the Black Books, and if it does, it cannot be cleared from your journal. **?**

[†](#note_13)The Boethiah Cultist in this random encounter doesn't become hostile until he's been very close to you for some time.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. An alias property needed to be adjusted to make sure he immediately attacks on sight.

[†](#note_14)Radiant world enounters for the Companions can cause the involved members to get pulled out of their normal crime factions which would then cause them to become permanently hostile to player werewolves even though they aren't supposed to be.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_15)Skjor will not be present for this random encounter after the Companions questline is finished, as he will be dead by then.

[†](#note_16)This random encounter is supposed to terminate after Miraak's death, but doesn't.

-  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_17)You cannot loot the shrouded armor set equipped on slain assassins in these random encounters.

[†](#note_18)This random encounter may give you a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") in The Rift even when it takes place in other holds.

- The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, addresses this issue. The aliases for the Dawnguard NPCs needed the WECrimeFactionAliasScript attached.

[†](#note_19)The encounter faction Orcs belong to for these random encounters against Forsworn is not set to be their enemies, so they never attack each other unless you initiate combat yourself.

- The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_20)The Vigilants will attack [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") on sight if they see him following you during [A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend"). Unfortunately, since Barbas is invulnerable, they will perish.

## Random Quest Encounters

These encounters and events occur as a result of actions taken during a quest, and they usually have a theme of revenge. Unless otherwise noted, the related quest must be completed.

| Encounter Name | Details | Options | Quest | Extra Requirements |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Afflicted Refugees Attack the Player** | Two [Afflicted Remnants](/wiki/Skyrim:Afflicted_Remnants "Skyrim:Afflicted Remnants") track and attack you. | Fight | [The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure") | None |
| **Alik'r Accusation**[†](#intnote_21) | Two [Alik'r warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") harass a [Redguard Woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Woman "Skyrim:Redguard Woman"). | You can talk to the woman afterwards, she will start the quest if you do not already have it. | After stage 0 but before stage 10 of [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need") (Two Alik'r having an argument with a Guard by Whiterun's gate) | None |
| **Bats!**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | A swarm of bats appears. | Stay calm or panic. | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)") | Between 10pm and 5am |
| **Blood Horker Revenge** | Two [Blood Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker") hunt you down because they want revenge. | Fight | [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") | None |
| **Disguised Vampire Lord**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | A [Traveler](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveler "Skyrim:Traveler") walks up to you and reveals himself to be a vampire. He summons a gargoyle and attacks. | Fight | [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") | In a [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities") or [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") |
| **Lost after the Wedding** | [Plautis Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Plautis_Carvain "Skyrim:Plautis Carvain") and his wife [Salonia Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Carvain "Skyrim:Salonia Carvain") are found with their gifts ransacked and their bodyguard absent after missing the [wedding](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death"). | Talk to them | [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") | None |
| **Louis Letrush vs Thug** | [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") being attacked by a [Thug](/wiki/Skyrim:Thug "Skyrim:Thug") sent by [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"). | Help him or watch | [Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep") | Louis still alive. Let Louis take [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") to end Promises to Keep |
| **[Magic Student](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Student "Skyrim:Magic Student")** | A [Student](/wiki/Skyrim:Student "Skyrim:Student") approaches and asks you for help training his wards. | You can choose to help or not. | [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") | None |
| **Morgrul *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Attack**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | Bandits hired by [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)") attack you. One bandit will have [a contract](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul%27s_Orders "Skyrim:Mogrul's Orders") to recover Mogrul's money from you. | Fight | [A New Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt") is in progress (Mogrul is alive and demanding money). | On Solstheim. |
| **Namira Cultist Offers the First Bite** | [Sigar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigar "Skyrim:Sigar") feeding on a dead female [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf"). | He offers you a bite which you can accept or decline. | [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") | None |
| **Necromancers Attack Player** | A [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") necromancer and a random race necromancer track you down and attempt to kill you. | Fight | [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star") | None |
| **Pilgrim visiting the tree in Whiterun**[†](#intnote_22) | [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") and her [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") traveling to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") to visit the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree. | Talk to them | [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature") | Restore the Gildergreen (this encounter will not happen if you returned with a sapling) |
| **Ramblings of a madman *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*** | A [madwoman](/wiki/Skyrim:Madwoman "Skyrim:Madwoman") asks you to use the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") on her. | Fulfill her strange request or refuse | Start [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness") (there are different dialogue options if the quest is completed) | Madwoman still alive |
| **Taron Dreth's revenge**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | [Taron Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Taron_Dreth "Skyrim:Taron Dreth") appears and wants to know where you found the Aetherium item you made at the [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge"), or how you know his name. He will always engage you in combat no matter what you tell him. | Fight | [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") | None |
| **The drunken dare** | [Deep-In-His-Cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep-In-His-Cups "Skyrim:Deep-In-His-Cups") appears and demands 10,000 gold. | Pay up, ask for a lower amount, or refuse. | [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember") | None |
| **Thief lock picking** | A [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Thief (Thieves Guild)") attempting to pick a locked door is discovered by guards. The guards will attack him and try to kill him. Sometimes he may escape into a house/shop. | Help kill the thief, or just loot his corpse. Chase him down and kill him if he entered a building, the guards will not and his presence interferes with merchants trading. | [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") | Level 5. Between 10pm and 4am |
| **Thug sent by Louis Letrush** | A [Thug](/wiki/Skyrim:Thug "Skyrim:Thug") may be sent by [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") for revenge after your betrayal. | Fight | [Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep") | Keep [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") to end Promises to Keep |
| **Torkild**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood") asks you to find [Torkild](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild "Skyrim:Torkild") during the quest [Filial Bonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Filial_Bonds "Skyrim:Filial Bonds"). This random encounter is unlocked and Torkild will appear at some point. He turns into a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear") and attacks when you speak to him. A [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild%27s_Letter_to_Wulf "Skyrim:Torkild's Letter to Wulf") will be found on his corpse. | Fight | [Filial Bonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Filial_Bonds "Skyrim:Filial Bonds") | Started [Filial Bonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Filial_Bonds "Skyrim:Filial Bonds") but have not advanced past stage 10 |
| **Vigilant Remains**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | The body of [Lynoit](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynoit "Skyrim:Lynoit") appears surrounded by the unlootable remains of three vampires. On his body is a [Dawnguard cache key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Cache_Key "Skyrim:Dawnguard Cache Key") and his [orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Orders_-_Lynoit "Skyrim:Dawnguard Orders - Lynoit") which reveal the location of three caches that can be looted. The caches should reset. | Loot Lynoit and raid the caches. | [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") or  [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") | None |
| **We Know...** | A [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") gives you a [strange letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(DB) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (DB)") written by the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). | Ask the courier who wrote the letter, then read it. | [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") | None |

[†](#note_21)This random encounter should not appear after the quest is completed for the Alik'r, but it still does.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.

[†](#note_22)This random encounter doesn't terminate once Ardwen and her dog reach [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"), as they'll stay there 24 hours a day.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Cut Encounters

These encounters were cut from the game. Not much else is known about them, including what your options would have been and what requirements you would have had to meet.

| Encounter Name | Details | Options | Requirements |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Escaped Prisoner | An [escaped prisoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Escaped_Prisoner "Skyrim:Unused NPCs") wandering the wilderness. | unknown | None |
| Nord Warrior | A [Nord warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Nord "Skyrim:Unused NPCs") wandering the wilderness. | unknown | unknown |
| `WEDL11` | Two Nord [Headsmen](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Headsman "Skyrim:Unused NPCs") patrolling the wilderness wearing executioner outfits and carrying headsman's axes. | unknown | unknown |

## Notes

- The dragon encounters are not in the *Random Quest Encounters* section because they are not a direct result of perceived actions during the Dragon Rising quest; rather, they are simply possible after the completion of that quest.
- Random vampire attacks on settlements (added by Dawnguard) are disabled in [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition") and the [Nintendo Switch version](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") of the game.

## Bugs

- Some random encounter trigger boxes have their script properties set to the wrong holds.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=22837))
- Even though random nighttime vampire attacks in settlements and cities is supposed to be disabled in the Special Edition, they can still happen after using Auriel's Bow on the sun. **?**
- Multiple random encounters may spawn in the same spot (such as bandits fighting a conjurer, plus Vigilants of Stendarr fighting skeletons) at the same time. **?**

# Skyrim:Worldspaces

## Overview

Blackreach

This page lists all the **worldspaces** in *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*. Worldspaces are continuous areas without doors between cells.

:    **[Alftand Cathedral](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Cathedral "Skyrim:Alftand Cathedral")** — A large Dwarven ruin southwest of Winterhold containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alftand)
:    **[Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small glade in a cavern east-southeast of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancestor+Glade+%28DG%29)
:   **[Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — Hermaeus Mora's plane of Oblivion.
:   **[Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior")** — A small alternate dimension within Azura's Star containing Malyn Varen and any Dremora that he summons.
:    **[Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — A haunted island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackbone+Isle+%28CC%29)
:   **[Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach")** — An immense, naturally lit cavern inhabited by hordes of Falmer and containing the ruins of a Dwemer city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackreach)
:    **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized cave southwest of Karthwasten along the banks of the Karth River containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
:    **[Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto")** — A small cave north of Falkreath containing animals and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloated+Man%27s+Grotto)
:   **[Boneyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneyard "Skyrim:Boneyard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — An enclosed graveyard in the Soul Cairn.
:    **[Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto")** — A small cave north of Solitude containing horkers or bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brinewater+Grotto)
:   **[Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small cave only accessible through Darkfall Cave serving as the only access to the Forgotten Vale.
:    **[Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass")** — A small cave south-southwest of Darkwater Crossing containing Falmer and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+Pass)
:   **[Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — The wilderness area surrounding Fort Dawnguard, accessed through a cave entrance southeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dayspring+Canyon+%28DG%29)
:   **[Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") — A plane of Oblivion belonging to Mehrunes Dagon.
:    **[Deepwood Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Vale "Skyrim:Deepwood Vale")** — A small valley far west of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deepwood+Redoubt)
:    **[Dragonsreach, Great Porch](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach,_Great_Porch "Skyrim:Dragonsreach, Great Porch")** — The residence of the Jarl of Whiterun Hold, the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
:    **[East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse")** — A warehouse on the Solitude docks immediately southeast of the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=East+Empire+Company+Warehouse)
:    **[Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary")** — A small underground grove and worship site of the followers of Kynareth south-southwest of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eldergleam+Sanctuary)
:    **[Emperor's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Emperor's Quarters")** — The personal transport vessel of the Emperor, Titus Mede II. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Katariah)
:    **[Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave")** — A small cave northeast of Riften containing leveled animals, frostbite spiders, and giants. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fallowstone+Cave)
:    **[Forebears' Holdout](/wiki/Skyrim:Forebears%27_Holdout "Skyrim:Forebears' Holdout")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small cave southeast of Dragon Bridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forebears%27+Holdout+%28DG%29)
:    **[Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — An isolated region in northwestern Skyrim once inhabited by the Snow Elves worshipping the god Auri-El. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forgotten+Vale+%28DG%29)
:    **[Frostmere Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Depths "Skyrim:Frostmere Depths")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin south-southwest of Dawnstar containing bandits and the unique wispmother the Pale Lady. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostmere+Crypt)
:    **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through Fallowstone Cave containing a giant whose tribe has defiled a shrine of Malacath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
:    **[Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") — A small island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Tooth+%28CC%29)
:    **[Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly")** — A self-contained worldspace far northeast of Skyrim containing Blood Horkers and their leader Haldyn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Japhet%27s+Folly)
:    **[Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire")** — A large Forsworn camp and cave east of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire)
:    **[Labyrinthian Chasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian_Chasm "Skyrim:Labyrinthian Chasm")** — A large Nordic ruin southeast of Morthal containing draugr, skeletons, trolls, wisps, and the dragon priest Morokei. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
:    **[Labyrinthian, Tribune](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian,_Tribune "Skyrim:Labyrinthian, Tribune")** — A large Nordic ruin southeast of Morthal containing draugr, skeletons, trolls, wisps, and the dragon priest Morokei. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
:    **[Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg")** — A small Nordic ruin northeast of Labyrinthian containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valkygg)
:    **[Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")** — A major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of High Rock, and the capital of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Markarth)
:   **[Misty Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Misty_Grove "Skyrim:Misty Grove")** — One of the Myriad Realms of Revelry created by Sanguine, where he is holding a feast with some of his followers.
:    **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern")** — A small, open-roofed cavernous grove lush with many kinds of flora and fungi, located due north of Hunter's Rest and northwest of Half-Moon Mill which is inhabited by bears and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moss+Mother+Cavern)
:    **[Red Eagle Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Ascent "Skyrim:Red Eagle Ascent")** — A small cave and two exterior camps east of Markarth containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Eagle+Redoubt)
:    **[Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")** — A major city in the southeast of Skyrim near the borders of Morrowind and Cyrodiil, and the capital of the Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riften)
:    **[Shadowgreen Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowgreen_Cavern "Skyrim:Shadowgreen Cavern")** — A small cave northwest of Solitude containing leveled spriggans and animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shadowgreen+Cavern)
:   **[Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze")** — A small Nordic ruin east of Labyrinthian containing atronachs and a dremora. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shalidor%27s+Maze)
:   **[Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn")** — A large Nordic ruin with a portal to Sovngarde containing draugr, dragons, and a dragon priest. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skuldafn)
:    **[Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")** — A major city on the northwest coast of Skyrim, and the capital of both Haafingar and the entire province. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude)
:   **[Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A plane of Oblivion haunted by lost souls.
:    **[Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum")** — A small cave southeast of Helgen containing the conjurer Bashnag and his coven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Southfringe+Sanctum)
:   **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)")** — The Nordic afterlife.
:   **[The Mind of a Madman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman")** — The mind of Pelagius the Mad.
:   **[Volkihar Courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — The courtyard attached to Castle Volkihar and Volkihar Keep.
:    **[Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")** — A major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun)
:    **[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")** — A major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the Dunmeth Pass to Morrowind, and the capital of Eastmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm)

## Notes

- The above list excludes the main **[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)")** and **[Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")** worldspaces and five test worldspaces ([Avoidance Exterior](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#CWTestHold "Skyrim:Test Cells"), [TestDLC1PlantWorld](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#TestMeganWorld "Skyrim:Test Cells")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), [The Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#WindhelmPitWorldspace "Skyrim:Test Cells"), [World of FX Light Regions](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#FXLightWorldSpace "Skyrim:Test Cells"), and the unnamed world [`CWSiegeTestWorld`](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#CWSiegeTestWorld "Skyrim:Test Cells")).
