# Skyrim:Wreck Of The Brinehammer

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png) | Shipwreck: Wreck Of The Brinehammer ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+Of+The+Brinehammer)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Father of the Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Father_Of_The_Niben "Skyrim:Father Of The Niben")* *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| Brinehammer01 BrinehammerExterior01 BrinehammerExterior02 | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| Northwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar")  Northeast of [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") | |

The Wreck Of The Brinehammer

The **Wreck Of The Brinehammer** is a [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") northwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") along the shore of the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts").

It has an [exterior](#Wreck_Of_The_Brinehammer)—the deck, cargo hold, and surrounding area—and one interior zone: *[The Brinehammer Below Deck](#The_Brinehammer_Below_Deck)*.

### Exterior and Cargo Hold

The exterior of the wrecked ship has very little to explore. Several [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") corpses float in the water to the north of the ship, amid some wreckage. To the southeast is a small pool filled with several [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). A [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") can be found immediately west of the ship, and another immediately to the north by a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"). Somewhat west of the ship is a third nirnroot and over a dozen [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") clusters. Further to the west on two small islands there are two more nirnroots, three [quicksilver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") and some stone ruins.

On the deck of the ship there are several [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"). Facing northwest, there is a structure with stairs leading down to a door to the interior of the ship. There is also a door leading to a cabin on deck open to the sky. In the cabin there is a skeleton on a bed, crushed by a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

It is also possible to enter the ship's interior via either of two doors located in the cargo hold, which itself is accessible by jumping up through a hole in the hull of the stricken vessel. The cargo hold is inhabited by a lone mudcrab and contains a skeleton on an unusable bedroll. Beside this is a crate with a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Father of the Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Father_Of_The_Niben "Skyrim:Father Of The Niben")* on top and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There are also two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and an adept-locked chest.

Underwater near the stern of the ship is an apprentice-locked chest.

### The Brinehammer Below Deck

The interior of the ship is inhabited by a few mudcrabs. It is in chaos below decks due to anything that wasn't secured being thrown around when the ship ran aground. There are numerous sacks of food found throughout the ship. Near the first mudcrab below deck and a [horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") mounted head amidships, a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")* can be found on the floor. There is a novice-locked door on your left. Continuing along the side of the starboard-side hull, there is another mudcrab concealed by a doorway into a cabin, and just after this is a lootable skeleton of an unfortunate person who was crushed by moving cargo. Past this towards the aft of the ship is a set of shelves holding two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") along with several pieces of [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots"): two [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), two [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), one [malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore"), one [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore"), one [moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone "Skyrim:Moonstone"), and one [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore"). At the front of the ship is a novice-locked door leading down to the cargo hold with a ramp up opposite to a storage area, where an open crate holds a selection of random strength [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"); two [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a [potion of waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing") and a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"). A second open crate holds two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and four bottles of wine.

Following the deck around to the port side, there is another mudcrab in the second section on your left. At the end of the passage is a cupboard on its side with seven [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on the shelves. There is also another skeleton that was crushed during the grounding. Just before this the passage is staggered to the left, where you will find an unlocked chest. To the right of this are two sets of shelves with ten common books, two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") either on the shelves or on floor in front of them. Between the shelves is a [shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth"). At the end is a dresser on its side containing common [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and a doorway into another passageway. There is the novice-locked door seen previously on your immediate left. Beyond this there are three stacks of three bunk beds built into the left-hand wall, with the bottom ones available to use. A dresser is between the first and second stacks, with a common book on the floor in front of it. The passage ends at an unlocked door leading down to the cargo hold with another mudcrab concealed in front of it.

## Notes

- You can swim underneath the wreck and enter the cargo hold through a hole in the hull by jumping from a certain angle.
- Southeast of the wreck, you can find an overturned skiff sheltering two mudcrabs. Underneath the boat you can find a knapsack containing some loot, and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") skill book *[Daughter of the Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Daughter_of_the_Niben "Skyrim:Daughter of the Niben")*.
- Iron and [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") ore veins can be found to the southeast and north-northwest of the ship, respectively.
- North-northwest of the ship, a locked chest underwater contains a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") skill book *[Sithis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sithis "Skyrim:Sithis")*.

## Bugs

- Various snags where you can be trapped and not get free without using console teleport commands exist around the edges of the Brinehammer, specifically where you walk up walls, etc.

# Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png) | Shipwreck: Wreck of the Icerunner ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Icerunner)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder"), [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| IcerunnerExterior01, IcerunnerExterior02, Icerunner01 | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") North of the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") | |

The Wreck of the Icerunner

The **Wreck of the Icerunner** is an Imperial ship which will run aground east of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") and the assassin [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"). It contains only one zone, *[Wreck of the Icerunner](#Wreck_of_the_Icerunner)*.

The ship was transporting passengers and cargo between Skyrim and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"). One notable passenger was [Daynas Valen](/wiki/Skyrim:Daynas_Valen "Skyrim:Daynas Valen"), who traveled on the ship from [Anvil](/wiki/Lore:Anvil "Lore:Anvil") to Solitude while researching the [Legend of Gauldur](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend"). During the quest [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"), the ship will be targeted by [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra"), Deeja, and their Blackblood Marauders. They will arrange for the light in the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse") to be extinguished and, once the ship has run aground, they will board the ship, massacre the crew, and steal all the cargo.

## Related Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.

### Exterior

When you approach the shipwreck there are four Blackblood Marauders who are not aggressive unless attacked, a melee marauder and archer on the deck, and on land, one magic user and one archer marauder. The magic user will greet you, inquiring whether it was you who put out the fire in the lighthouse, and inform you that Deeja is in the hold, down two decks. By the bottom of the gangplank there is a barrel, sack, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). In the water between the beach and wreck, there is a dead sailor along with three visible barrels, a sunken barrel, and an empty chest. On the starboard side of the wreck there is a sunken apprentice-locked chest and two sacks, but be aware there are two [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") that will attack. There are two rowboats drawn up on the beach, the first of which has three sacks and an open crate containing a leveled healing potion, a leveled stamina potion, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and four bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"). The second rowboat has four sacks, a satchel, a barrel, a medium coin purse, and a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). On the beach near the rowboats are two barrels, one of which has a sack and two coin purses on top—one large and one small. There are also three more sacks, an apothecary's satchel, a leveled helmet, and a random variant of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"). If you enter the wreck without killing the marauders, and then proceed to clear out below deck, when you return three of them will have gone taking everything above, not in the water with them and leaving just the archer marauder and an empty rowboat behind. On the beach in and around the wreck you will find two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") plants, four [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Everything that will disappear with the marauders is marked as owned and therefore stealing when taken.

On the deck, there are two dead Imperial soldiers, one by the wheel and the other by the rear mast. There is also a dead sailor on the east (port) side of the deck. Also on the port side are three hanging, harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and two barrels containing common food. On the west (starboard) side is a sack, a rowboat containing five sacks, a barrel, a leveled shield, a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"), two coin purses (one medium, one large), two potions, and a novice-locked chest. Next to this rowboat are two more sacks, two barrels, and a leveled helmet. This rowboat and everything around it will also have been taken if the marauders aren't dealt with before going inside. Finally there are five barrels around the cabin.

### Wreck of the Icerunner

Upon entering there are seven sacks including one on a shelf of a cupboard, and an open crate containing two loose gold. Down the stairs there are two bookcases, seven more sacks, and a barrel. On your right is an open door to a bedroom containing a magic using marauder, an empty chest, a cupboard, and a table holding two common books. Following the corridor around, there is a sack, a dead sailor, an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") and a cupboard with a further three sacks on its shelves. Around the corner to the left is a melee marauder sitting on a bench by a closed door. This opens into the dining room, with three long tables. There are four loose coins on one of these tables. There is also a cupboard with a satchel, an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), three bottles of Nord mead and two bottles of Alto wine. Beside the cupboard is an open crate containing one bottle of Alto wine and two bottles of Nord mead. Hanging at the back of the room are two samples of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, and a portion of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Back out to the corridor and there are three more open doors on the right leading to bedrooms. There is nothing of interest in the first room. The second has a dead sailor, an [Imperial light shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Light Shield"), a small table with a copy of the book *[Chance's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Chance%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Chance's Folly")* on it, an iron helmet on a bed post, a copy of the book *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")* on the second bed, and an empty chest. The third bedroom has a pair of leveled boots in front of a wardrobe, an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") on the floor, and a small table with a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Outside of this bedroom is a table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") next to a copy of *[Biography of Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v1")*. Next to this is a bookcase with a sack and eighteen [common books](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_2 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 2") on its shelves. Opposite the second bedroom is a closed door leading on and into a storage area. There is a Blackblood Marauder sitting behind the door at a table holding three sacks and an apothecary's satchel. In the storage area there are a total of six barrels, nineteen more sacks, a dresser, a cupboard, a knapsack, a dead Imperial soldier, an Imperial sword and shield, a cupboard, and a large and two small shelving units.

Down another flight of stairs into the hold with shallow water, there are twelve sacks and nine barrels scattered about, as well as another satchel. There is another marauder over by a closed door leading to the room containing Deeja. In the room with Deeja are two empty chests, two potions, three sacks, a barrel, a leveled helmet, and a third Imperial light shield.

## Notes

- The wreck will not exist prior to stage 125 of Lights Out!.
- Iron and [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") ore veins can be found to the east and south-southwest of the shipwreck, respectively.
- Lights Out! originally had a scenario where you could help [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka") and [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") get rid of the Blackblood Marauders. In this scenario, Aldis would help you defeat the marauders on the ship. The dialogue branch `MS07DeejaBleedout` and related dialogue for Aldis indicate Deeja could either be killed or spared. If she was spared, Aldis would ensure she was imprisoned. It's unknown what would've transpired afterward.

The Wreck of the Icerunner

The **Wreck of the Icerunner** is an Imperial ship which will run aground east of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") and the assassin [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"). It contains only one zone, *[Wreck of the Icerunner](#Wreck_of_the_Icerunner)*.

The ship was transporting passengers and cargo between Skyrim and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"). One notable passenger was [Daynas Valen](/wiki/Skyrim:Daynas_Valen "Skyrim:Daynas Valen"), who traveled on the ship from [Anvil](/wiki/Lore:Anvil "Lore:Anvil") to Solitude while researching the [Legend of Gauldur](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend"). During the quest [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"), the ship will be targeted by [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra"), Deeja, and their Blackblood Marauders. They will arrange for the light in the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse") to be extinguished and, once the ship has run aground, they will board the ship, massacre the crew, and steal all the cargo.

## Related Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.

### Exterior

When you approach the shipwreck there are four Blackblood Marauders who are not aggressive unless attacked, a melee marauder and archer on the deck, and on land, one magic user and one archer marauder. The magic user will greet you, inquiring whether it was you who put out the fire in the lighthouse, and inform you that Deeja is in the hold, down two decks. By the bottom of the gangplank there is a barrel, sack, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). In the water between the beach and wreck, there is a dead sailor along with three visible barrels, a sunken barrel, and an empty chest. On the starboard side of the wreck there is a sunken apprentice-locked chest and two sacks, but be aware there are two [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") that will attack. There are two rowboats drawn up on the beach, the first of which has three sacks and an open crate containing a leveled healing potion, a leveled stamina potion, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and four bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"). The second rowboat has four sacks, a satchel, a barrel, a medium coin purse, and a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). On the beach near the rowboats are two barrels, one of which has a sack and two coin purses on top—one large and one small. There are also three more sacks, an apothecary's satchel, a leveled helmet, and a random variant of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"). If you enter the wreck without killing the marauders, and then proceed to clear out below deck, when you return three of them will have gone taking everything above, not in the water with them and leaving just the archer marauder and an empty rowboat behind. On the beach in and around the wreck you will find two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") plants, four [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Everything that will disappear with the marauders is marked as owned and therefore stealing when taken.

On the deck, there are two dead Imperial soldiers, one by the wheel and the other by the rear mast. There is also a dead sailor on the east (port) side of the deck. Also on the port side are three hanging, harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and two barrels containing common food. On the west (starboard) side is a sack, a rowboat containing five sacks, a barrel, a leveled shield, a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"), two coin purses (one medium, one large), two potions, and a novice-locked chest. Next to this rowboat are two more sacks, two barrels, and a leveled helmet. This rowboat and everything around it will also have been taken if the marauders aren't dealt with before going inside. Finally there are five barrels around the cabin.

### Wreck of the Icerunner

Upon entering there are seven sacks including one on a shelf of a cupboard, and an open crate containing two loose gold. Down the stairs there are two bookcases, seven more sacks, and a barrel. On your right is an open door to a bedroom containing a magic using marauder, an empty chest, a cupboard, and a table holding two common books. Following the corridor around, there is a sack, a dead sailor, an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") and a cupboard with a further three sacks on its shelves. Around the corner to the left is a melee marauder sitting on a bench by a closed door. This opens into the dining room, with three long tables. There are four loose coins on one of these tables. There is also a cupboard with a satchel, an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), three bottles of Nord mead and two bottles of Alto wine. Beside the cupboard is an open crate containing one bottle of Alto wine and two bottles of Nord mead. Hanging at the back of the room are two samples of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, and a portion of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Back out to the corridor and there are three more open doors on the right leading to bedrooms. There is nothing of interest in the first room. The second has a dead sailor, an [Imperial light shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Light Shield"), a small table with a copy of the book *[Chance's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Chance%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Chance's Folly")* on it, an iron helmet on a bed post, a copy of the book *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")* on the second bed, and an empty chest. The third bedroom has a pair of leveled boots in front of a wardrobe, an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") on the floor, and a small table with a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Outside of this bedroom is a table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") next to a copy of *[Biography of Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v1")*. Next to this is a bookcase with a sack and eighteen [common books](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_2 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 2") on its shelves. Opposite the second bedroom is a closed door leading on and into a storage area. There is a Blackblood Marauder sitting behind the door at a table holding three sacks and an apothecary's satchel. In the storage area there are a total of six barrels, nineteen more sacks, a dresser, a cupboard, a knapsack, a dead Imperial soldier, an Imperial sword and shield, a cupboard, and a large and two small shelving units.

Down another flight of stairs into the hold with shallow water, there are twelve sacks and nine barrels scattered about, as well as another satchel. There is another marauder over by a closed door leading to the room containing Deeja. In the room with Deeja are two empty chests, two potions, three sacks, a barrel, a leveled helmet, and a third Imperial light shield.

## Notes

- The wreck will not exist prior to stage 125 of Lights Out!.
- Iron and [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") ore veins can be found to the east and south-southwest of the shipwreck, respectively.
- Lights Out! originally had a scenario where you could help [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka") and [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") get rid of the Blackblood Marauders. In this scenario, Aldis would help you defeat the marauders on the ship. The dialogue branch `MS07DeejaBleedout` and related dialogue for Aldis indicate Deeja could either be killed or spared. If she was spared, Aldis would ensure she was imprisoned. It's unknown what would've transpired afterward.
